1933.07.25

Negotiating Handover Procedures 1

Li Jichun Discusses Matters for Three Hours at the Two Commissioners' Residence

Tao Shangming Sets Off This Morning with the Four County Magistrates of Northern Ping

Song Naigan Fails to Take Over the Tangshan Public Security Bureau Yesterday

(Tangshan) The Tangshan Municipal Public Security Bureau has decided to implement the takeover on the 25th, with no further delays. This afternoon, Li Jichun went to the Qixin Company to discuss matters with the two Commissioners, Xue and Lei, for three hours before leaving. In the evening, a banquet was held for Song Naigan and Gao Xixian, the new and old Bureau Chiefs, to introduce them to each other. The outcome was harmonious, and a smooth exchange is expected. (24th Dispatch)

(Tangshan) According to the two Commissioners, Xue and Lei, speaking to reporters, the takeover can begin as soon as the county magistrates arrive in Tangshan, with no other issues. (24th Dispatch)

(Beiping) After arriving in Tangshan, Song Naigan has met with Li Jichun to negotiate the takeover procedures thoroughly. It is expected that the takeover can be completed today or tomorrow. The county magistrates of Luan Dong and Luan Xi counties can gather in Tangshan today. The takeover will begin from tomorrow onwards. The special police officers preparing to be brought must have their handover procedures thoroughly negotiated before proceeding to avoid misunderstandings. Tao Shangming previously agreed with Yuan Liang to select one hundred police officers from Ping to form a special police force. He will lead them to the northern route tomorrow morning to negotiate the takeover. If there are no obstacles, Miyun and Wanping will be taken over around the 26th, Jixian will be taken over on the 27th, and it is scheduled to be completed by the 28th. (24th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Song Naigan arrived in Tangshan yesterday and contacted Li Jichun, intending to take over the Public Security Bureau according to the original agreed plan. Li Jichun stated that the original police and garrison forces in Tangshan could not be withdrawn temporarily and would be withdrawn on the 24th to be replaced by the police led by Song. From this morning until noon, Li had not sent anyone to notify. As of this time, the Tangshan Public Security Bureau has not yet been taken over. Xue Zhiheng, our resident commissioner in Tangshan, inquired with Li, who stated that he would hand it over as soon as the procedures were completed. Today, the citizens of Tangshan gathered near the Public Security Bureau, wanting to witness the appearance of the Blue Sky White Sun flag, but they were disappointed again. It is currently rumored in Tangshan that agents of the puppet government have arrived in Tangshan to obstruct the takeover, attempting to delay it with excuses. Whether there will be a postponement will be reported later tonight. (24th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Tao Shangming is scheduled to lead the four county magistrates of northern Ping tomorrow morning to first contact the Japanese army in Miyun, and then separately go to Huairou, Zunhua, Miyun, and Jixian counties to take over. He will also travel with one hundred Beiping security police officers. Tao stated that the takeover affairs of the four counties in northern Ping have been coordinated with the Japanese military and can proceed smoothly. Shi Yousan's troops have withdrawn from the railway line and have been transferred to Yutian for concentration. When traveling near Yutian, there was a misunderstanding with the local militia, which was quickly resolved. (24th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The puppet troops along the Lutai-Ludong railway line were completely withdrawn yesterday and concentrated in Tangshan to await reorganization. The puppet troops in Ninghe are also gradually decreasing and will be completely withdrawn soon. (24th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The education associations of various counties in the war zone have submitted a request to the military sub-committee, requesting that the various troops return the military advances, vehicles, and livestock. (24th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Bank of China remitted 200,000 yuan to Tangshan on the 24th, which is for the Li unit's post-war expenses. (24th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Tangshan Special Public Security Bureau was originally scheduled to be taken over yesterday, but due to incomplete procedures, it has been changed to today. The Japanese and puppet troops from the three counties of Linyu, Luanxian, and others will withdraw successively tomorrow and will be taken over. Li Zeyi will lead the remaining ten county magistrates and 500 Tianjin security police officers directly to the various counties to take over, without concentrating in Tangshan. All funds have been handed over to Li Jichun for distribution. (24th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Li Zeyi returned to Ping from Tangshan this afternoon with Japanese military officer Shibayama. According to reports, the handover of war zone affairs is proceeding smoothly and no complications have occurred. The puppet troops will be concentrated in Tangshan from today to be counted and await being incorporated. He came to report everything to He and Huang. He also visited Yu Xuezhong in Tianjin. Because everything was in order, Colonel Shibayama also had no need to stay in Tangshan and returned to Ping on the same train. (24th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The progress of taking over the Ludong war zone is quite slow. Yesterday afternoon, a new Chinese county magistrate arrived in Tangshan and discussed matters with Li Jichun. As a result, it was decided to take over the public security bureau and county government this morning, and it was decided to take over Ninghe, Yutian, Fengrun, Luzhou, Laoting, Qian'an, Lulong, Funing, and Changli tomorrow. The Beining Railway Bureau has been ordered to prepare trains to transport the dismissed subordinates of Li Jichun. Currently, the takeover of Miyun and other places must be delayed slightly. Today, the county magistrates of Miyun, Jixian, Zunhua, Huairou, and other places north of Beiping have arrived here one after another. They will go to Miyun to take over on Tuesday. (24th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Tangshan Public Security Bureau Chief Song Naigan failed to take over on the 24th. It is reported that there are still unresolved issues with the reorganization of Li's troops, and the takeover of various counties must be postponed for another day or two. (24th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Xue Zhiheng came to Tianjin to urge the payment of funds and returned to Tangshan on the evening of the 23rd. Li Jichun hosted a lunch banquet for the new and old public security bureau chiefs, Song Naigan and Gao Xixian, on the 24th to discuss the handover. Song intends to take over on the morning of the 25th, but it is unknown if it can be done. (24th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Yu Xuezhong convened the newly appointed public security bureau chiefs of the war zone for a briefing on the morning of the 24th. Yu originally planned to go to Gan on the 24th, but due to issues with Li's troops, he will still be unable to depart on the 25th. (24th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The provincial government has decided to first establish a war zone security team with a total force stationed in Fengrun and Luzhou, and the organization will begin on the 24th. (24th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The High Court will send personnel to restore the High Court branch office after taking over Luxian. (24th Dispatch)

Li Jichun's Remarks 2

Reorganization to be Implemented Tomorrow

Reorganization can be Completed in Three Days

Tangshan, 24th Morning - A reporter interviewed Li Jichun at the Jiaotong University headquarters. Li stated that the reorganization is scheduled to be implemented from the 26th and can be completed within three days. He has already sent personnel to begin the work. The general headquarters' political affairs office has been concluded, and tax collection in various counties has also been ordered to cease. However, tax collection in Tangshan City is still ongoing to compensate for the debts incurred after arriving in Tangshan, and it will stop after the province sends personnel to Tangshan to take over. The takeover of the various counties will be implemented as soon as the provincial county magistrates arrive. He will be absolutely responsible to ensure that no problems occur and has ordered preparations for the handover. Li also stated that the army's doctrine is quite bright and upright, and he personally has no desire for leadership or fame and fortune. He has also never abandoned the Republic of China. His aim is to save the country and the people, and he does not care about outside criticism or praise. He will be vindicated after the fact. (24th Dispatch)

Aviation Expert Returned from Germany

Sun Tonggang Flies to Beijing 8

= Took off from Fürth, Germany on the 26th of last month =

= The journey was over 20,000 miles and took a total of 28 days =

Many Hardships Endured Along the Way

Will Fly to Jinan Tomorrow to Visit Family

(Nanjing) Sun Tonggang, an overseas Chinese aviator who studied in Germany, flew his self-funded plane from Germany on the 26th of last month, passing through Austria's Ber, Grlitz, Yugoslavia, Turkey's , Afghanistan, Persia, India's , and Myanmar and Siam's Menggu. He arrived in Annam this month on the 20th, flew to Guangzhou the next day, arrived in Changsha on the 23rd, and flew to Beijing from Changsha today, landing at Ming Palace Airfield at 2:30 PM. At 8 PM, the Beijing press corps hosted a dinner at the Central Hotel to welcome Sun. Sun's father is in Jinan, and he plans to fly to Jinan on the 25th to visit him. According to reports, apart from Chen Wenlin, he is the second Chinese person to fly solo for a long distance. It took a total of 28 days from Germany to Beijing, with only 19 days of flying and 10 days and five hours of stopping. There were a total of fifteen stops. The report stated that he originally intended to donate this plane to the National Government, but after reconsidering that the plane can only carry one person and might not be suitable for the talents in the country and would be ineffective, and that he might still take this plane back to Germany to study aircraft engineering for further development, he was unable to donate the plane at this time. (24th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Sun Tonggang, a young Chinese aviator who studied in Germany, took off from Futh, Germany on June 26th in his self-prepared single-seat Klem aircraft to return to China, crossing Europe and Asia, passing through more than a dozen countries. He arrived in Guangzhou on July 20th after many hardships along the way. He arrived in Changsha on the 23rd and flew to Beijing on the afternoon of the 24th, landing at Ming Palace Airfield. Sun is the first person to fly solo from Europe back to China. He encountered danger many times along the way and almost died. Fortunately, Sun was able to repair the aircraft himself and completed his journey according to the original plan. At a time when the country is in urgent need, Sun has brought glory to the country by advocating for aviation to save the country and is truly admirable. When Sun arrived in Beijing, he circled the sky three times before landing on the ground. Many agencies and organizations did not arrive at the airport to welcome him because they did not know that Mr. Sun was flying so fast. Only a small number of agency representatives, organizations, the press, and others were waiting at the airport. After Sun got off the plane, he shook hands with the welcomers and was led to the stationmaster's office by Director Du to rest. Then, a cadre from the Lizi Society welcomed him to stay at the society. Sun is healthy and energetic and tirelessly talked about his flight. According to reports, it took 28 days from taking off from Fürth, Germany on June 26th to arriving in Beijing on the 24th, with 16 days of flying, a total of 130 hours, and a distance of more than 20,000 miles. He passed through more than a dozen countries, including Austria, Hungary, Bulgaria, Czechoslovakia, Turkey, Arabia, Persia, India, Burma, Siam, and Annam to reach Guangzhou. He encountered difficulties when passing through deserts and wetlands. When passing through Arabia, he encountered a very high tornado and was forced to land in the desert three times. He got lost midway, the plane was burned, and he flew the damaged plane to Baghdad in Arabia. It could not be repaired there, so he flew more than a thousand miles to Basrah, where he was able to repair it. The local British garrison was deeply impressed by the spirit of the Chinese people and gave him preferential treatment. Later, on the way from Persia to India, when passing through a high mountain 100 miles from Calcutta, he encountered a rainstorm, and the plane's engine stopped due to the rain. He landed on a small mountain to repair it himself. That night, he risked arriving in Calcutta, where the Chinese Consul stationed in Calcutta and 500 overseas Chinese, and 1,000 British people came to the airport to welcome him. He stopped for two days and flew to Yangon. On the way, the motor leaked oil and he was forced to land. He arrived in Yangon on July 13th and was welcomed by overseas Chinese and the authorities. Continuing to fly to Bangkok, he encountered heavy rain again on the way to Annam. The clouds were high and the mountains were steep, so he turned back and landed in Pakse. He was detained by the French garrison for two days. Later, the French garrison was released after receiving a reply from General Fache, the French garrison. He flew to Hanoi and continued to fly after the Hanoi airfield was bad, part of the plane was burned again, and he continued to fly, 20 meters above the ground. The tail of the plane suddenly broke, and the plane was out of control. At that time, more than 200 people at the airport lost their color. Re-landing in the field, French garrison commander Lager Fache personally expressed his admiration and condolences, and ordered the railway workers in the garrison to repair it. He flew to Hanoi and arrived in Guangzhou on the 20th, Changsha on the 23rd, and finally the capital on the 24th. Sun led reporters to visit the plane, which is a wooden Klem-style monoplane painted yellow, named "Aviation to Save the Country". The tail has a party emblem on one side and a national flag on the other. The plane weighs 456 kilograms, has a load of 235 kilograms, has 90 horsepower, and flies at 145 to 175 kilometers per hour. The cost is 20,000 yuan. The fuselage is very small and can only accommodate one person. Sun is from Jiahe, Hebei, 26 years old, the younger brother of Sun Tongxuan, commander of the 26th division. After graduating from middle school, he served in the army. In the 17th year, the government sent him to study in Germany, where he entered the Klem factory and Siemens factory for a year of internship and studied at the German Aviation School, Sports Aircraft School, National Aviation School, Gliding Aircraft School, and finally entered the National Jiaotong Aviation School, specializing in heavy aircraft. He graduated this year. Sun believes that China has a vast territory and aviation is still in its infancy. To resist foreign aggression, we must actively build air defense. Since September 18th, his ambition has become more firm. He took advantage of the three-month vacation after graduating from the Jiaotong Aviation School to fly back to China, so that our blue and white national emblem can soar in the alien sky. Sun plans to fly to Jinan on the 25th to visit his father. After the vacation, he will return to Germany to study aircraft manufacturing at the university. On the evening of the 24th, the capital's press held a grand banquet to welcome him. (24th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Current Commentary

The Sino-Soviet Negotiation on the Chinese Eastern Railway and the Reality of Far Eastern Peace 15

Since Japan withdrew from the League of Nations, it has gained military advantages to realize its decades-long ambition to dominate the East Asian continent. However, diplomatically, it has been isolated. Britain, originally Japan's ally, had very close relations with Japan in terms of political interests in the Far East, and their stances on the Soviet Union were also quite consistent. However, with the rise of the economic bloc movement, Japan, seeking to control the Far East, first advocated the so-called "Japan-Manchukuo Alliance" and then subtly implied its opposition to Europe and the United States. Therefore, cracks had long existed between Britain and Japan. Recently, since the failure of the World Economic Conference, the contradictions between international cooperation and national economic protectionism have become increasingly apparent. Major countries have all devoted themselves to national protection and self-defense. Japan's foreign policy has also undergone a fundamental shift. Although it can no longer afford to engage in conflict with Britain, it is already in a hostile position with Britain in the markets of Southeast Asia and India. And in North Manchuria with the Soviet Union, the situation is even more acute. Now, the world knows that the Soviet Union and Japan's puppet state are conducting negotiations in Tokyo on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway. The Soviet Union, on the surface, continues to maintain its peaceful stance, expressing its willingness to sell it at a reasonable price. Japan and its puppet state, on the other hand, are seeking to expand their military strength in the Northeast and to economically erode the Chinese Eastern Railway, subjecting it to the dual control of the Japanese army and the "South Manchuria Railway," hoping to seize the Chinese Eastern Railway at a low price.

The reason for actively seizing the Chinese Eastern Railway, even before the completion of the Jihui Railway, Yanji-Sanxing Railway, and Labin Railway, is that all countries in the world are striving for their own domestic development, and internationally, they are mostly focused on self-sufficiency and striving to strengthen their military preparations. During this period, Japan, seeing the effectiveness of its aggressive policies, wants to implement further aggression. The previous so-called military actions were still justified by the pretext of preventing communism and maintaining peace in the Far East. Now, they say that the period of temporary handling of the military situation in the three northeastern provinces has passed. From now on, they will permanently station troops in the Northeast and establish standing divisions. The number of troops and the location of the headquarters have not been determined, but it is undoubtedly clear that they intend to permanently station a large number of troops in the Northeast, build fortifications within our three eastern provinces and Jehol, and prepare for future international wars. This is one aspect of Japan's active preparation for war. Furthermore, Japan's budget this year allocated only 448 million yen for army expenditures and 375 million yen for the navy. However, the military budget for next year, although the figures have not been determined, the army's demand will be no less than 550 million yen, and the navy has a new warship construction plan, the cost of which is expected to exceed 600 million yen. Just looking at the army and navy expenditures, it is not just a quasi-wartime budget but is advancing to a wartime budget. This is the second aspect of Japan's active preparation for war. Currently, Japan's overseas expansion, although it can be considered successful in the Northeast, still cannot solve its urgent needs, and the promising markets of India and Southeast Asia are all

restricted by the economic bloc within the British Empire. Therefore, they are still paying attention to the mainland of our country, expanding their economic influence on one hand and provoking political disputes on the other, threatening us to stop technical cooperation with the League of Nations so that they can seize the opportunity to monopolize it. This is the third aspect of Japan's active preparation for war. We are well aware that Japan, as a maritime power, has a strong army not directed at the Soviet Union but at our country. Now, they are using the Chinese Eastern Railway issue as a wedge, locking down Manchuria in the west and sealing off Suifenhe in the east, and engaging in various kinds of propaganda against the Soviet Union, saying that the Soviet Red Army is actively deploying in Eastern Siberia, which they can use as an excuse to massively increase troops in the four northeastern provinces. This is the fourth aspect of Japan's active preparation for war.

Given these four aspects, although Sino-Japanese relations have temporarily eased due to the North China Agreement, Japan's policy towards China has not changed. The so-called peace is merely a deceptive term for diplomatic purposes.

Recess Period of World Economic Conference 18

Hull Will Propose a Limit of Three Months

Major Deletions to the Economic Report

Currency Committee Met in Detail Yesterday

(London) At the final meeting of the World Economic Conference on July 27, the US chief delegate, Hull, will propose in his speech that the recess period be approximately a maximum of three months. It is heard that Hull's proposal, presented at the plenary meeting of the Economic Committee last week, was well received. His proposal argues that the governments of the countries attending the World Economic Conference should, during the recess period, undertake to establish an agreement to no longer set up new trade barriers and agree to gradually reduce existing barriers. However, any agreement on stopping the setting up of new barriers may be subject to reservation conditions, such as the imposition of taxes on dumped goods. It also advocates that this agreement should be observed by the governments of the countries. Once the governments of the countries accounting for fifty percent of world international trade have accepted it, it will be implemented, and its effective period is indefinite, but it can be terminated one year after implementation with one month's notice. (Reuters telegram from the 23rd)

(London) The economic part of the World Economic Conference has concluded, and the currency part awaits the opening of the plenary session, so the representatives now have time to attend to their private affairs. The revised report of the Economic Committee has removed some of the language extravagantly describing its achievements. When the Currency Committee met today, the chairman, Cox, presented the achievements of the committee somewhat lavishly, but it is feared that the plenary session will follow the example of the Economic Committee, and the optimistic conclusions in the report will be deleted. The wheat agreement seemed very likely to be concluded last week, but the atmosphere today is rather bleak. However, Chairman Morgenthau is not yet pessimistic. The US dollar opened at 4 shillings and 6.4 pence on the London foreign exchange market, then fell to 4 shillings and 7 pence, and finally returned to 4 shillings and 6.8 pence. (Reuters telegram from the 24th) (London) The core committee of the presidium of the Economic Conference met at 10 a.m., chaired by British Prime Minister MacDonald, to determine the proposals to be submitted to the plenary session of the presidium tomorrow afternoon. After the meeting, the general impression was that MacDonald strongly advocated stipulating the procedures for resuming the work of the Economic Conference. This procedure should clearly define the timing of the second session of the Economic Conference, which seems to be determined by the core committee. The core committee is composed of the chair and vice-chair of the Economic Conference, the chair and vice-chair of the Currency and Economic Committees, and the rapporteurs. (Havas telegram from the 24th)

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Announces

Full Text of the Silver Agreement 19

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs will release the full text of the Nine-Power Silver Agreement, which was signed in London the day before yesterday, at 2 p.m. on the 24th. It has six articles. (Central News Agency telegram from the 24th)

(Nanjing) The Silver Agreement was signed in London on the 22nd. It is now known that the full text is as follows: India, China, and Spain, countries with silver reserves, and Mexico, the United States, Canada, Peru, Bolivia, Australia, and Japan, major silver-producing countries, because the governments of India and Spain are willing to sell a portion of their silver reserves, and because major silver-producing countries absorb raw silver into their treasuries to offset the silver being sold, which is beneficial to the major silver-producing countries, and because the sale of silver obtained from currency can be offset by the aforementioned purchase, to obtain stable silver prices, which is beneficial to China, and because the amount of silver sold from currency is limited in accordance with the following articles, an agreement is hereby established as follows: (1) The Indian government agrees that the amount sold annually in 1934 shall average 35 million fine ounces. The total amount of silver sold within four years from January 1, 1934, shall not exceed 140 million fine ounces. If the number sold in a certain year is less than 35 million fine ounces, it may be sold in subsequent years, but the total amount sold each year shall be limited to 50 million fine ounces. The above clause does not apply to India's sale of silver to any government for the purpose of reselling US bonds. (2) Major silver-producing countries shall not sell silver during the period to which this agreement applies and shall purchase a total of 35 million fine ounces annually from the raw silver of their mineral production starting in 1934. (3) The raw silver purchased in the above item shall be placed in the national treasury within the four-year period of this item for various monetary purposes, or for simple preservation. (4) The Chinese government agrees not to sell the raw silver obtained from melting down currency for a period of four years from January 1, 1934. (5) The Spanish government or the Bank of Spain agrees not to sell more than 5 million fine ounces of raw silver annually for a period of four years from January 1, 1934. (6) This agreement shall take effect from the date of ratification after acceptance by the governments of the countries and must be ratified before April 1, 1934. However, each ratifying country shall still be effective if it is prepared to purchase the stipulated amount of silver in accordance with the method of the above-mentioned second clause, even if one or more major silver-producing countries have not ratified it at that time. Any government that notifies that it has taken the necessary positive actions to implement the purpose of this agreement, this notification shall be regarded as a ratification document. Also, the US government should take the necessary steps to complete the plan of this agreement. (Central News Agency telegram from the 24th)

Establishment of Silver Agreement

All Parties Express Satisfaction 20

Believe it Will Greatly Benefit

Increasing Trade and Raising Silver Prices

(London) After the establishment of the Silver Agreement, all parties involved are extremely satisfied. The US delegation believes that the signing of the agreement will greatly benefit the improvement of global commerce and the increase of silver prices. The Canadian delegation believes that Canada is a silver-producing country, so it goes without saying that it will obtain direct benefits after the agreement is established, and the purchasing power of the Far Eastern countries will also increase as a result, which is especially beneficial to Canada. Indian people believe that the content of the agreement is quite beneficial to India, because according to the agreement, India can sell a portion of its silver reserves without causing silver prices to fall. Regarding this, the Chinese representative believes that the volatility of silver prices is extremely harmful to the development of international trade, and this agreement is a tool to prevent volatility. (Havas telegram from the 23rd)

Yan Huiqing Signed the First Word Last 21

(London) One of the clear results of the World Economic Conference is seen in the Silver Agreement today. The agreement stipulates that India's silver sales will be limited to 35 million ounces per year and Spain's to 5 million ounces per year within four years starting from January 1, 1934. At the same time, silver-producing countries must purchase 35 million ounces of mined silver annually. Everyone is very satisfied with this agreement. Pittman said today that this is the greatest event of his life. Negotiations were conducted throughout yesterday, and unanimous agreement was almost reached in the evening. The representatives then adjourned, and the agreement was slightly revised orally to allow each representative to sign the first word. All representatives except Chinese Dr. Yan Huiqing had signed the first word last night. Everyone then went to find Dr. Yan, and finally Pittman's secretary returned this morning with the document signed by Dr. Yan. (Reuters telegram from the 23rd)

Bombay Stock Exchange Was Once Excited 22

The report of the Bombay Silver Agreement caused excitement in the gold and silver exchange here, resulting in midnight trading. The bulls were elated and hastily raised silver prices by two rupees without studying the detailed meaning of the new plan. After the detailed telegram was published, it was realized that the silver position in the monetary world had changed very little, and the bulls were disappointed. Although the market had closed, they still sold what they had bought last night, causing the market price to fall again. The local market is watching and waiting for the reaction of other markets. According to business people, the Bombay silver furnace can barely cope with more than 35 million ounces per year, and the average amount of silver sold by the Indian government in the past from destroyed currency has never exceeded 35 million ounces either. (Reuters telegram from the 24th)

Roosevelt

Allows Gold Dollar to Fluctuate 23

Temporarily No Steps to Stabilize

Rumors of US Treasury Secretary Woodin Resigning

(Washington) Although there are widespread rumors tonight that some bankers and people in the securities industry have anticipated that the US government will announce its attitude towards further inflating the currency soon, those close to the government say that it is heard that the US president intends to temporarily allow the gold dollar to fluctuate and will wait until prices reach a satisfactory level and seem to be stable before seeking to stabilize the gold dollar. At that time, only redefining the gold content of the gold dollar will be the basis for stabilization. Furthermore, the president has not yet implemented any real or substantial inflation. The current currency trend is entirely to tighten industry and commerce. Therefore, Senator Thomas, who had previously drafted an amendment authorizing the president to redefine the value of the gold dollar, today advised the president to begin substantive inflation so that wheat prices could rise to $1.50. According to Thomas, the inflation of the currency so far has been entirely psychological. Even if the government authorizes the Federal Reserve to purchase national securities and implement unemployment reduction and construction plans, slightly inflating credit (i.e., lending), the increase in the prices of goods and securities is largely due to the general expectation of inflation rather than real inflation. The plan he has planned authorized the president to issue national circulation notes of 300,000 million yuan, and the time to start issuing them has now arrived. Although abandoning the gold standard and accepting silver for the repayment of war debts has caused the gold dollar exchange rate to plummet, he still does not consider it a real currency inflation plan. (National News Agency telegram from the 23rd)

As for the rumors that Secretary of State Hull and the US president have disagreements, they are gradually dying down. Central · National Government

Two Memorial Week Reports 34

Ye Chu Cang ·· Conscience and Capability

Zhang Ji ·· How to Consolidate the Party Foundation

(Nanjing) The National Government held a memorial week at 9:00 AM on the 24th. Over 400 people attended, including Lin Xiang, Li Yuanding, He Yaozu, Lu Chao, Wei Huai, and staff of the National Government. Chairman Lin led the ceremony. National Government member Lai Chu Cang reported, roughly stating that recently, various counties in eastern Henan have begun to be taken over, the puppet army has been reorganized, and the river water has receded. The situation seems to be easing, but in reality, it is still serious. It would be most dangerous if the people's morale were to relax as a result. As the saying goes, "Closing the door after the thief has left" implies blaming someone for not preparing in advance. However, if the thief has not left and the door is still not closed, it is even worse. There are many ways to prepare, but the most important is to strengthen human resources. The starting point for strengthening human resources is to seek the enrichment of the "heart" first. The scorching heat is oppressive, and actions are difficult. If an emergency occurs, one should still get up and dress, even if it is more tiring than usual, yet one does not feel the heat. This is driven by one's capability. Even in the depths of winter, one often feels shivering. However, if someone suddenly points out one's wrongdoing, the shame is overwhelming, and one's face will turn red and sweat. This is due to the function of conscience. Based on this conscience and capability, expanding and developing it is the way to enrich one's inner strength. In the Party anthem written by the Premier, there is a phrase "swear to be diligent and brave." The word "diligent" is the foundation for developing one's capability. The meaning of diligence seems ordinary, but it is not easy to put into practice. It is already difficult to find someone with diligent training among ordinary people. We are in difficult times and should put more effort into "diligence" to strengthen human resources. Then, financial and material resources will follow. I urge myself to be diligent and encourage my comrades with this. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 24th)

(Nanjing) The Central Government held a memorial week at 8:00 AM on the 24th. Chen Guofu, Zhang Ji, Xiao Jishan, Huang Jichen, Zheng Zhannan, Wang Qi, Ji Ciwen, and all staff members attended. Chairman Chen Guofu presided, and Zhang Ji reported, roughly stating that he has been traveling frequently in North China recently and has many feelings about what he has witnessed. The national crisis is serious and has reached its extreme. Generally, people blame the Party, saying that the measures are not good. At the same time, some comrades within the Party are also losing confidence. It should be known that the country's current situation is not the fault of the Party, nor is it the mistake of the revolution. It is truly because the people have not worked hard to follow the Premier's teachings and build the country according to the Three Principles of the People. Recently, some people have advocated opening up political power and implementing the Premier's founding program, which instructs us to return political power to the people, not to hand over political power to a few politicians and ambitious individuals, calling it "open." What benefit would this bring to the country? Recently, all reactionaries have taken the opportunity to attack, and the Party's foundation is becoming increasingly shaky. All comrades of the Party must uphold a spirit of perseverance and fortitude. (1) The Party is a revolutionary party, not a political party. Therefore, it is extremely important to restore the revolutionary spirit, strictly abide by the Premier's teachings, and fight to the end. (2) Correct erroneous views on life, cultivate a spirit of hard work and self-encouragement, not avoid difficulties, go deep into the countryside, promote the ideology, and do practical construction work. Only then can we talk about consolidating the Party's foundation and revitalizing the country. Time is pressing, and we cannot afford to hesitate any longer. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 24th)

Disposal of Income from the Zhengtai Railway

Ministry of Railways Rejects Belgian Proposal 46

(Nanjing) An official from the Ministry of Railways stated that the French loan contract for the Zhengtai Railway had expired, and the loan had also been repaid at the same time. Therefore, the Ministry of Railways sent personnel to take back the railway on December 25th of last year and manage it themselves. After taking over, the Ministry of Railways, due to the need for funds for the Huayin and Weinan sections of the Longhai Railway, ordered the Zhengtai Railway to allocate 100,000 yuan per month for a period of eight months, using the funds previously used to repay the principal and interest of the French loan to expand the Longhai Railway. This does not affect the Belgian company's loan guarantee. The construction costs of the Longhai Railway were also borrowed from the Belgian company. Now, because the income of the Longhai Railway is not strong, the interest on the loan from the Belgian company has also been delayed for a long time. Now that our country is willing to use the surplus from another railway to expand the Longhai Railway, the intention is to increase the income of the Longhai Railway in order to reorganize the old debt of the Longhai Railway. Although the Belgian company is well aware that this move does not affect its interests, it fears that the income of the Zhengtai Railway will decrease in the future, and it will have nothing to rely on. Therefore, under the pretext that the loan contract has expired, it demands that our country recognize the company as the first creditor, and that the income of the railway bureau must be used to pay the principal and interest of the company's loan first. Only if there is a surplus can it be used for other purposes. Its intention is nothing more than to oppose our country's independent disposal of the railway's income. The Ministry of Railways has already refuted this based on reason. Although the company still insists, it may not persist to the end. (Special dispatch from the 24th)

Longhai Railway Actively Completes Tongguan-Xi'an Section 74

Traffic Can Open by June Next Year

(Xuzhou) Ling Hongxun, Director of the Tongguan-Xi'an Section Engineering Bureau of the Longhai Railway, passed through Xuzhou from Zhengzhou to Beijing on the evening of the 23rd. According to him, in order to develop the northwest, the central government has specially instructed the Ministry of Railways to complete the Tongguan-Xi'an section of the Longhai Railway. The Ministry of Railways is currently negotiating with banks to borrow funds to build the section from Tongguan to Xi'an and has ordered materials from France, which will arrive in September. Laying of rails will begin in October, and traffic will open to Weinan this year. The roadbed of this section has been completed. At the same time, bids will be invited to continue building dams and bridges. The roadbed to Xi'an will be laid in February next year, and traffic can open to Xi'an in June. This section is a total of 130 kilometers and has no mountains to block it, only a few bridges to erect, so the project is relatively easy to estimate. The cost of this section, including locomotives, is 13 million yuan. In addition to the Ministry of Railways raising funds, the Beining Railway will provide 100,000 yuan per month. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 23rd)

Post's Round-the-World Flight Achievement 79

Reuters New York, the 23rd, when Post's plane arrived at Bennet Airport last night, the first to shake hands with him to congratulate him was Getty, who flew with him two years ago. When the Winnie Mae aircraft came to a stop, Post immediately stood up and waved to the more than 50,000 people welcoming him at the airport. Afterward, he was exhausted and fell down. He was then helped out of the plane and taken to his residence. Post later told people that if the weather was good, he could have flown around the world in four and a half days. Italian Aviation Minister General Balbo also intended to come to the airport to welcome him, but he arrived too late due to traffic congestion along the way.

榆林 80

Around 2 PM on the 20th of this month, areas outside Zhenchengkou, including Yidaohezi, Xijiawan, and Gucheng Beach, suffered hailstorms accompanied by heavy thunderstorms. Crops were severely damaged, and leaves were scattered everywhere. Farmers, distressed by this major disaster and anticipating reduced summer harvests, flocked to the county government to request inspections and relief measures.

Zhenchuan 81

Since the beginning of this year, the rains have been adequate in our fort, and the crops are growing well. The people are delighted and expect a bumper harvest. Unexpectedly, around 4 PM on the 21st day of the leap fifth month of the lunar calendar, dark clouds gathered, and the darkness was extreme. Lightning flashed, and thunder roared. In an instant, heavy rain fell, and after a few minutes, it turned into hail, some pieces as large as apricots and others as small as beans. The crops suffered greatly, and the damage was significant.

Dingbian 82

Tang Zhongfu, a representative of the people of Dingbian County, recently came to the province to appeal for aid. He reported that since the 13th year of the Republic [1924], droughts have followed one after another, resulting in labor without harvest. In the 17th year [1928], strong yellow winds howled, and not a drop of rain fell. At that time, sixty to seventy percent of the people fled. In the 19th year [1930], they suffered from rat infestations, making the scene even more tragic. As a result, two-thirds to three-quarters of the people lost their property and became displaced. In the past two years, there have been signs of severe drought. Crops in the fields have been abandoned after sowing. Living people have turned to death, and piles of white bones have formed. The death rate is incalculable.

###中部

In中部 on June 9th, at 4 p.m., black clouds gathered and thunder rumbled faintly. In an instant, a hailstorm broke out, with pieces like chicken eggs and small stones, accumulating to over a foot deep on the ground. Wheat ears were broken, broad beans were destroyed, and there was no hope for the autumn harvest. Mournful cries of the people were everywhere, truly pitiful. The county magistrate, Wei Jichuan, has already petitioned the provincial relief committee for aid.

Shangxian 83

The county magistrate of Shangxian recently reported to the provincial government that on the 9th, 10th, and 11th days of the fifth month, there was rapid lightning, strong winds, and torrential rain, mixed with hail. The hail was as small as chicken egg yolks or walnuts, and as large as rice bowls. All mature wheat and beans, as well as early autumn crops, were beaten into the mud. Fifty-five people and seventy-four cattle were killed. Furthermore, due to the disaster caused by this hailstorm, people lacked the means to survive. Some entire families were begging at the same time, while others were committing suicide by jumping into wells. The suffering was so terrible that one could not bear to witness it. He pleaded for the swift allocation of large sums of money and the dispatch of personnel to provide relief. The provincial government, upon hearing the news, has instructed the provincial relief committee to investigate and handle the matter.

Zhashui 84

On the evening of the 18th day of the fifth month, a sudden gale arose in the county, followed by hail as large as fists. This lasted for four hours, causing mountain torrents to erupt. Not only was the nearly ripe wheat crop completely submerged, but the newly sown corn and potatoes were also washed away, roots and all. Livestock and homes were washed away without a trace. The disaster victims are crying out in hunger, awaiting urgent relief.

Pingli 85

The areas of Lianxian River, Qiuhai River, and Songshan River in the eastern district, as well as Da Xiang River, Longdong River, Zhengyang River, Zhengzhong River, Chuangshi River, Nanxi River, and Baxian River in the southern district, suffered a disastrous hailstorm on the 18th day of the leap fifth month of the lunar calendar. The hail was as large as fists, weighing about half a catty [approximately 0.5 pounds]. Lasting for an hour, the crops were completely destroyed. The relief sub-committee has already submitted a report to the provincial authorities requesting relief.

Baoji 86

In the 11th, 12th, and 13th districts of Baoji, the barley harvest has failed, and the disaster situation is severe, especially in the 13th district. Most of the people have fled, leaving the land covered in dense grass. The villages are half-ruined. Another hailstorm has destroyed the autumn crops. More than two-thirds of the households have fled. The county magistrate has petitioned the provincial relief committee to provide swift relief. (July 20th)

武昌掘金案審查將完竣 87

The Investigation of the Wuchang Gold Digging Case is Nearing Completion 88

= New gold cellars were discovered in the gold digging site, but there was nothing inside. Another gold cellar was discovered in the Liushi area of Huangkang County =

(Hankou Correspondence) The gold cellar dispute at Kong Geng's residence in Wuchang, which was triggered by the encroachment and unauthorized digging by his neighbor, Peng Younan, has caused a major controversy. The entire committee of the investigation team inspected the cellar site and unearthed two thousand taels of silver ingots and fragmented silver. A new cellar was also discovered. At that time, Kong Geng disputed the ownership issue with the investigation committee, leading to the entire committee resigning in anger and requesting the garrison headquarters to select new committee members to take over. The original report stated, "The committee members, following your instructions, organized a gold digging investigation committee, which was established on the 12th of this month and commenced work. All progress has been reported to you in person. Currently, obstacles have arisen in the course of the investigation, and the committee members are unable to fulfill their responsibilities due to a lack of competence. After a meeting, it was decided that all members will resign collectively, which is recorded in the minutes. Therefore, we submit this document for your review and approval to select new members to take over, which would be more convenient." The so-called obstacles likely refer to the prevention of excavation by the Kong family. Kong insisted on ownership, while the investigation committee argued for the right to discovery. Neither side would concede, resulting in a stalemate. However, although Kong is disputing ownership, it is still for the purpose of overseeing distribution and for public benefit, not for personal gain. The investigation committee members were nominated by various agencies and organizations and have no intention of personal enrichment. Therefore, although there are disagreements, they can be easily explained. On the 20th, the police department instructed all investigation committee members, stating, "The committee has been established for a week, and although there is no concrete solution to the case, a general outline has emerged. Continuing the investigation will lead to an early conclusion. Further changes will increase the difficulty of gathering evidence. The committee members were selected by various government offices and legal groups to uphold justice. Avoiding difficulties and seeking comfort is unacceptable. Recently, news media have been critical. To respect public opinion and the plaintiff's altruistic intentions, you are requested to jointly assume responsibility and actively handle the matter fairly, without hesitation. Your resignation is rejected." At the same time, Kong Geng published a notice in various newspapers, stating that he had not changed his original stance. The investigation committee then announced their reinstatement and decided to excavate the new cellar on the 21st, which Kong also supported. At 2 PM that afternoon, the committee members, including Yu Jusun, and Zhou, the director of the Fourth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, led several police officers to the cellar site and ordered workers to excavate. Kong also invited Jin Jutang, the chief of staff of the Garrison Department, to supervise in person to ensure caution. Unexpectedly, after excavation, the so-called new cellar contained no gold, silver, or treasures, only scattered bricks and piles of soil. The investigation committee, believing that the mystery had been solved and that further investigation was unnecessary, requested the Garrison Department and the Public Security Bureau to immediately withdraw the guarding troops and police. They then consulted and decided to strictly investigate Peng Younan's unauthorized digging, based on the original plan. It is said that the committee had already gathered a great deal of evidence on this matter, but the discovery of the new cellar caused complications. It is now scheduled to hold another investigation meeting on the 24th, at which a decision will be made. The conclusion of the case is not far off.

While the gold cellar dispute at the Kong residence was unfolding, another incident of gold cellar discovery occurred in Liujiaxia Bay, Yangying Ridge, Huangkang County. The excavated items included thirteen catties of red gold, which were also hidden by Liu Changmao (Liu Weizhen). Liu was originally from Huangkang but resided in Wuchang. Both places contained many hidden treasures. The simultaneous discovery of two gold cellars is considered a rare event. The discoverer of the Huangkang gold cellar was Liu Genius, a member of the Liu clan. (July 21st)

無錫 99

Wuxi 100

特院通緝韓案綁匪 101

Special Court Issues Arrest Warrant for Kidnappers in the Han Case 102

In the case of Han Wentai, the head of Xu Xie Township (Yangming Township) in the third district, who was kidnapped and tragically killed by bandits, the Public Security Bureau's detective team captured seven kidnappers, including Li Zhiping, at the Yuchun Teahouse in Shanghai. Li Zhiping and Yuan Yonghe were escorted back to Wuxi from Shanghai by court police officer Chen Zuosheng, accompanied by the political affairs police chief Wu Zhengrong, and were interrogated and detained by the County Court Procuratorate. The remaining five, including Jiang Hanchen, were not brought back to Wuxi. It is now known that during the third court hearing at the Shanghai First Special District Court on the 21st of this month, Jiang Hanchen was absent due to illness. His lawyer, Zhuang Chengyi, appeared in court to defend him. Ni Jingqing, the owner of Chenghe Porcelain Shop in Shanghai and Jiang's guarantor, requested to withdraw his guarantee in court due to the seriousness of the case. Lawyer Zhuang persuaded him to continue as the guarantor. For the sake of caution, he also assigned four shop assistants to take turns guarding Jiang to prevent his escape and avoid suffering heavy losses. Unexpectedly, Jiang took advantage of the shop assistants' deep sleep around 3 AM that night and managed to climb onto the roof and descend using a telephone pole, escaping without a trace. After being discovered, it was too late to catch him. The guarantor, Ni Jingqing, was shocked and immediately reported the escape to the Special District Court, requesting his arrest. After receiving the report, the Special Court, believing that Jiang's escape indicated a strong suspicion in the Han Wentai case, ordered his arrest. Chen Fugen, Ding Fugui, Jin Hengpei, and Hu Shifu, who were released, have not been apprehended despite repeated orders from the police. They remain at large, which is extremely egregious. The Court has also instructed its subordinates to issue a unified arrest warrant and requested public security agencies in various counties to assist in their apprehension for interrogation and trial. County Magistrate Yan Shenyu of this county, considering the importance of this case, will bring Li Zhiping and Yuan Yonghe, who have already been escorted back to Wuxi, to the county government within the next few days for questioning with Yang Abao and Zhou Shungen, in order to investigate the matter thoroughly.

六月飛雪之奇聞 103

Strange News of Snow in June 104

Since the beginning of summer, the weather in our county has been extremely dry and hot, with the Fahrenheit temperature reaching around 100 degrees. In the past two days, there has been a slight drizzle, and the weather has become somewhat cooler. Unexpectedly, around 3 PM the day before yesterday in Ge Da Bridge, Kaihua Township, 14th District of the county, snow suddenly began to fall from the sky for about 10 minutes, but the snowflakes were very thin and small. At the time, dark clouds covered the sky, and the weather was suddenly colder than usual. The local residents were amazed.

京市財局科員遇仙人跳 105

Official of the Nanjing Finance Bureau Falls Victim to a "Honey Trap" 106

Zhang Zongren, a first-class clerk from the Nanjing Finance Bureau, a native of Jiangpu, and 38 years old, came to Wuxi to play with his fellow villagers, Chen Zhuping and others, on the 17th of this month. The day before yesterday afternoon, they went to the park in the city center to drink tea. Shen Keqin, a well-known local rogue and member of the "Eight Gang," was experiencing financial difficulties and discussed with his wife, Hua Fengying, imitating the "honey trap" technique from Shanghai to extort money. Fengying, who was 29 years old and possessed beauty comparable to Pan An and Xi Shi, happened to meet Zhang Zongren in the park that day. She sent him flirtatious glances and conveyed affection with her eyes. Zhang, suddenly seeing a beautiful woman's favor, was so captivated that he thought he was dreaming. They began to pour out their hearts to each other, then hired a car to tour the lake and mountains, whispering sweet nothings, almost wanting to ascend to immortality. That evening, the two went to room 42 of the Dadong Inn, hoping to consummate their relationship. However, just as Fengying was half-heartedly resisting, Shen Keqin and several of his accomplices broke down the door and entered. Fengying feigned panic, while Shen pinned Zhang down and demanded money. Unable to resolve the situation, they were taken to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau, where Director Wang held a preliminary hearing and, considering Zhang's status as a public official and his reputation, persuaded them to settle. Zhang paid 50 yuan to resolve the matter. It is said that Zhang's uncle works for the Nanjing City Party Headquarters. Upon hearing the news, he was furious and intends to come to Wuxi to investigate the truth and file a lawsuit to punish Shen.

常熟公安長警請願索餉 107

The bureau then released 15,000 yuan as a temporary measure. Now, another half-month has passed, and the meager amount is insufficient to sustain them. Many have accumulated debts and pawned their clothing. The officers of each branch bureau find it unbearable to continue in this situation. They are planning to jointly petition the authorities for their back pay to maintain their livelihoods.

六合淫婦受辱自盡 113

A Lehe Adulteress Commits Suicide After Being Humiliated 114

In Lehe County city there is a boathouse on Banbianhe owned by Jiang Ronghe, whose wife, Song, is still young. She is inherently lewd and, since Jiang is out at sea with the boat, she can't stand being alone. She first became acquainted with Zhao Mazi, Sun Aizi, and Jiang Sanlong, who came and went frequently without interruption. Last month Zhao and Song quarreled over a trivial matter and broke up. On the 19th, Zhao suddenly came to Song's house. Neighbor Zheng scolded Song for her lack of affection, declaring that he would interfere if she abandoned Zhao. Sun and Jiang also arrived one after another. The three adulterers quarreled with each other. Jiang Ronghe learned of this and was furious. He scolded Song for not keeping her wifely duty. Unable to bear this humiliation, she conceived a desperate plan, secretly taking opium to commit suicide. When discovered, doctors were called to treat her, but she died. Zhao Mazi, seeing that he had caused the trouble, fled without a trace. Jiang Sanlong then purchased a coffin and collected the body.

高郵趙梅春遭匪慘殺 117

Zhao Meichun of Gaoyou Brutally Killed by Bandits 118

Zhao Meichun, a farmer from Zhu Xie Village, Tenth District of the county, has little property, only a few acres of land. Previously, the bandits had demanded money from him, ordering him to hand over 300 yuan within a week. Zhao borrowed everywhere, but only managed to borrow 80 yuan. When the bandits came to collect the money on the due date, Zhao handed over the borrowed money and knelt down to beg for mercy. The bandits were furious and shot him dead. How tragic.

皖匪搶刦糧船傷人 119

Anhui Bandits Rob Grain Boats, Injuring People 120

Jin Gou Town, in the 12th district of our county, borders Anhui Province. A gang of over 100 bandits from Anhui suddenly arrived the other day, armed with guns, and robbed more than 30 grain boats. 杭州湖濱旅館中之棄嬰案 121

Abandoned Baby Case in a Lakeside Hotel in Hangzhou 122

Two female guests, Shi Jingwen and Li Zhongzhi, arrived at the Lakeside Hotel in Hangzhou yesterday. They had an infant wrapped in swaddling clothes and a rattan basket. They booked room number 33 and went to bed with the door closed that night. The next morning, they went out together, leaving the child in the room. The hotel staff initially paid no attention. When they had not returned by noon, suspicions arose. They searched the room and found a note and three silver dollars. The note instructed the staff to send the child to Mrs. Zuo at No. 1 Yingshi Road, West Street. The hotel staff followed the instructions and sent the child to Mrs. Zuo, but Mrs. Zuo refused to accept the child. She said she would contact her when Zhongwei returned to Hangzhou. The child is now temporarily being cared for by Ms. Xu, another female guest in the hotel. This is also a strange and twisted case.

湖墅發生刦案 123

Robbery Occurs in Hushu 124

Wang Changquan, a resident of No. 24 Huian Qiao, Daguan, Hushu, Hangzhou, who formerly served as the manager of the Hangzhou factory of Sanyou Industrial Society and is currently the manager of the Reformatory, had a small fortune. Last night (23rd) at 9:40 PM, six bandits speaking in the dialect of northern Jiangsu broke into his home. Two bandits were unarmed, and four were armed with guns. They first drove all the members of the Wang family into one room and began to search for valuables. They then fled toward Xiaohe. The victim found that the stolen items included nine gold rings, two gold watches, two platinum watches, one pair of gold earrings, a total of 119 yuan in cash, and one pair of leather shoes.

明光張八嶺管轄問題 125

Jurisdiction Issues of Zhangbaling, Mingguang 126

Zhangbaling (i.e., Sandu, Liubao) in Chuzhou originally belonged to the jurisdiction of Jashan New County, as documented by provincial and central authorities. However, local gentry strongly objected, and the dispute remained unresolved. Now, due to business tax collection issues, the Chuzhou County government has requested instructions from the headquarters. The headquarters has issued an order stating that, according to the provincial government's reply, the gentry of the fort have deep-seated territorial prejudices. The allocation will be made after amicable guidance. Temporarily, it remains under the jurisdiction of Chuzhou County.

Therefore, we earnestly request your approval and prompt action. The revival of the nation depends on it. We respectfully submit this to you, awaiting your reply."

Authorities Decide on Steps to Handle the "Tunan" Ship Sinking Incident 136

Serious Negotiations Will Be Initiated After Handling Post-Disaster Matters 138

滬靑兩海員會昨均通電力爭招商局 139

Shanghai and Qingdao Seamen's Associations Both Telegraphed Yesterday, Arguing with China Merchants Bureau 140

The "Tunan" ship, which was owned by the China Merchants Bureau and was sailing from Yantai to Dalian, was sunk by the "Changchun Maru" of the Japanese-owned Dalian Mail Steamship Company in the waters of Shandong. The China Merchants Bureau quickly handled the aftermath and provided relief to the victims. It is now learned that the Ministry of Communications has decided on two steps to handle this matter. In addition, the Special Party Branch of the Chinese Seamen and the Qingdao Seamen's Union telegraphed yesterday, requesting the authorities to conduct serious negotiations and provide generous compensation to the victims. The details are as follows:

决定處置步驟 141

Decided Handling Steps 142

After the "Tunan" ship was sunk by the "Changchun Maru," the Ministry of Communications, after receiving the report, dispatched Gao Tingzi, the director of the Navigation Administration Department, to Shanghai to investigate the truth. He has already returned to the Ministry with a detailed report on the incident. It is now learned that the Ministry of Communications has decided on two steps to handle this matter: The first step is to order the China Merchants Bureau to handle the post-disaster matters for the passengers and crew, such as issuing compensation. After the first step is completed, the second step of negotiations will begin. First, the China Merchants Bureau will negotiate compensation with the Dalian Company. If the company evades responsibility or the negotiations are unsuccessful, the Ministry will request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a protest with the Japanese side. As for the cargo carried by the ship, it will be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Maritime Law to ensure that the passengers do not suffer losses.

海員黨部通電 143

Seamen's Party Branch Cables 144

The Shanghai District Preparatory Office of the Special Party Branch of the Chinese Seamen cabled yesterday: "All levels of seamen's unions, newspapers, and organizations, please note that the state-run China Merchants Bureau's 'Tunan' ship was sunk by the Japanese ship 'Changchun Maru' in Shandong waters, and most of the crew members drowned. The tragedy is self-evident. We believe that our colleagues in the shipping industry, who serve amidst the turbulent waves, cannot avoid such misfortune in reality. However, the authorities of the China Merchants Bureau should work with our leading seamen's organizations to jointly plan for the aftermath, which would be legitimate. However, the bureau has completely entrusted the handling of the affairs of the victims to the Jun'an Society, which has already been explicitly revoked, and is attempting to perfunctorily fulfill its responsibilities by citing the precedent of Xin Kang. Such mistreatment of seamen and disregard for human life not only chills the hearts of our colleagues in the shipping industry but also causes deep resentment among the public. Based on the party's position, this office has (1) presented a letter to the higher party department, (a) sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, adopting effective methods to stop the illegal activities of the Jun'an Society, (2) sent a letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, lodging a serious protest with Japan for compensation for losses and guaranteeing that similar incidents will not occur in the future, (3) sent a letter to the Ministry of Communications, requesting that the China Merchants Bureau generously compensate the families of the victims. We hereby telegraph, vowing to resolutely oppose the China Merchants Bureau's perfunctory approach. We hope that all sectors of the country will unite to support us in order to value human life. The Shanghai District Preparatory Office of the Special Party Branch of the Chinese Seamen."

Although a small number of people were fortunate enough to survive, they are living a miserable existence without adequate relief. The tragic situation is chilling to those who hear of it. We have suffered from continuous internal wars and frequent foreign aggressions in recent years. The lives of our people are as cheap as ants, and our territory is at the mercy of others. The sinking of the 'Tunan' has caused an unprecedented and tragic event, which is due to the weakness of our country and the poverty of our people. In this situation, if we do not take immediate and satisfactory action, not only will the dead be gone, but we, the living, will become the successors of the 'Tunan.' Therefore, after mourning, this union dares to propose three measures: (1) Request the authorities to investigate the truth and conduct serious negotiations. (2) Provide compensation to the families of the deceased. (3) Provide relief to the survivors and compensate them for their losses. In short, we must ensure that the dead rest in peace, the living are safe, and those who have suffered losses receive adequate compensation. Otherwise, this union, leading all the seamen of Qingdao, under the leadership of your union, vows to support this case until a satisfactory outcome is achieved. The telegram is urgent, and we await your instructions."

Unprecedented in the Same Month for Nearly a Century 162

Since its establishment in late August of the 20th year of the Republic [1931], the main work of the National Government Flood Relief Committee has been the three urgent tasks of industrial, agricultural, and social reconstruction, all of which are managed by Zhu Ziqiao, the director of the Disaster Area Working Group of the Committee. Regarding the industrial reconstruction part, the Committee hired Xi Dejiong as the director of the Industrial Reconstruction Office, who worked hard to repair the main dikes of the Jianghuai, Ganhan, Yiluo and Yun rivers. He recently returned to Shanghai and reported the details to Director Zhu, who was very gratified. The water level in one part of the Han River reached 47 feet and 2 inches. The torrents were surging, and the situation was dangerous. The dikes repaired by our Committee were originally designed to exceed the 20-year flood level by three feet. This time, the water rose, and the dikes were still 4-5 feet and 7-8 feet above the water surface. The dikes were able to be preserved, and the survivors were spared from suffering another disaster. I was very relieved to hear this. Your director has been in charge of the industrial reconstruction work of this group, and your guidance has been excellent. Especially during the emergency of flood prevention, you were able to be stationed in Hanzhong to plan and prevent the situation, taking responsibility bravely. The dikes in Jianli, Jialu, Huangmei, and the Mahua dike at the junction of Anhui, Hubei, and Jiangxi were either affected by bandits during the construction or suffered other failures, resulting in dikes that were not up to standard and in danger. However, thanks to effective flood control and rescue, they were not damaged. As for the small dikes along the rivers owned by the people, which are not within the scope of industrial reconstruction, even if there are overflows, they have not caused major disasters.
