Page 13

The Agony of Late Spring and Mosquito Control Qingqu

It used to be said in the Spring and Autumn Annals, "Heaven does not cease winter because of human dislike for its cold." Now, I'll twist that and say, "Why doesn't Heaven cease summer because of human dislike for its heat?" I imagine everyone, amidst the intense heat and oppressive glare, would agree. Although some might say summer is still better than the cold of winter, because the number of people who can wear heavy furs, use stoves, and live in warm, enclosed rooms is ultimately small. Yet, those who brave frost and snow, enduring hardship, number in the thousands. Not seeing the heavy snow and the huddled figures on the streets, they often get invaded by the cold air at night, resulting in freezing and death on the roads? Then, according to this, even though the heat of summer is high, the general poor people actually benefit quite a bit, living the most comfortable life even while sleeping outdoors.

However, this is only looking at one aspect. If we truly distinguish between advantages and disadvantages, the height of summer is a great enemy of human life. Why? Once the scorching heat arrives, everyone feels somewhat impatient. Speaking lightly, the tiny mosquitoes, born with sharp mouths, when you are tired and want to enjoy a peaceful sleep, they buzz and buzz, disturbing your dreams. Not only do they disrupt your sleep, but they also suck your blood. If you don't swat them until their bodies are like powder, the mosquitoes' bellies will be full, like a red gauze lantern, and finally they will fly away, calling out, "Are you awake yet?" The other day, a friend of mine had an interesting discussion about mosquitoes. Someone advised him to buy a box of Pig Brand mosquito incense, ensuring they would all be killed and he wouldn't suffer from them. Unexpectedly, this friend disagreed greatly. He said, I would never use Japanese products to harm Chinese mosquitoes. I would rather let mosquitoes suck my blood than listen to the Japanese bring my life, alas! These few words truly have a sense of humor, worthy of contemplation!

In fact, getting rid of mosquitoes is not difficult. If there are no weeds in the courtyard and no stagnant water, these eggs will not breed. Even the water tank used daily is most likely to breed mosquitoes. However, to eliminate their seeds, simply take a few snails and raise them in the water, and the wrigglers in the tank will disappear. The interior is generally cleaner. If it's not a bustling market, bedbugs would not usually visit. The only suffering is from mosquitoes, but with careful prevention, these insects are not impossible to get rid of. Even flies, if you pay attention to cleanliness, will have no way to invade, leading to harm to hygiene. As for the annoyance of heat, if you don't feel hot in your heart, you won't sweat profusely. As the saying goes, "A calm heart naturally feels cool." This shows the relationship between psychology and physiology. Sometimes, when the heat is extreme, try thinking of the scene of "high terrace blowing evening wind, white moon shining on the east eaves, arranging new melodies in front of the door, clear light filling the jade zither, looking up at solitary geese flying, listening to the mournful chirping of crickets," and you will naturally feel a cool breeze, caressing my arms, as if transported to a cool world, a different realm altogether, how joyful! Summer Cultivation Rongyu

The weather is so hot, the sun spreads out like a fiery canopy; the water in the small river is scorched, raising small bubbles, as if boiling. At this time, the villagers, both men and women, must go to the fields to work. The lush green rice seedlings are already over a foot tall, arranged neatly. They need the sun to shine on them to grow. They need water for irrigation to prevent withering. They also need human fertilizer to nourish them to thrive. Moreover, they need to have the weeds removed to grow peacefully. Farmers, to adapt to their environment, or rather, hoping for a good harvest, wear bamboo hats, go barefoot, and work in the fields under the scorching sun. The water in the rice fields feels boiling hot. There are also leeches and water leeches desperately trying to bite you. Sweat pours out all over the body, like a fountain. The skin is tanned as dark as a bronze statue. Weeding, pulling grass, and pumping water occupy their days. They don't even have time to take a nap or fan themselves, doing their work desperately. If the harvest is good, they can keep some rice for themselves. If they encounter floods, droughts, or locust plagues, all they get is hard work and wasted effort. It is truly "After gathering nectar from a hundred flowers to make honey, for whom do they toil, for whom do they busy themselves?" Worthy of farmers' lament!

Although cotton is not as troublesome as rice, the soil often needs to be loosened. This loosening work is done slowly, hoeing around the roots, not recklessly like a large-scale project. There is also the removal of weeds, working every two or three days. The hotter the weather, the faster the weeds grow, and the busier the weeding work becomes. Under the scorching sun, women wrap towels around their heads; men wear bamboo hats, also working desperately. "People do not know the hardship of farmers, assuming the grain in the fields grows by itself." City dwellers obtain things easily, but do not know the difficulty of farming. When you have time, please visit the countryside to see for yourself, then you will know "Each grain in the daily meal is the result of hard work!" Cold Words Yu Youqing

People sitting under electric fans complain about the heat, and rickshaw pullers pulling carts on the streets also complain about the heat. This is the equality of heat, without distinction between rich and poor.

Fashionable young ladies showing their legs and coolies baring their torsos are the same, indicating the initial stage of equal rights for men and women. People sleeping in silk-screened rooms may not be as comfortable and sweet as those sleeping on cement floors, which has a philosophical meaning.

A woman's face only has red, white, and black: red lips, white face, black hair and eyebrows. The Northeast Fourth Company Commander Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twelve

Poor and lowly suffer hardship enlisting in the army; a sick man who falls behind willingly resigns; a sentimental soldier

If I were Yang Guizhi, I would definitely be thinking like this in my heart: Zhao's family should come to propose marriage that day, they should come to formally engage that day, and they should choose a wedding date that day. For someone about to become a bride, these are the things one inevitably imagines. However, if I don't go back, wouldn't that mean he couldn't solve the first riddle, and wouldn't he be greatly disappointed? I know about the Yang family's affairs. In this marriage, Guizhi herself can make half the decisions. Now, if Guizhi is offended, then this matter will be mostly difficult to succeed. In the event that things go wrong, wouldn't that fit the saying, "The cooked duck has flown away." Thinking like this, he couldn't put it out of his mind, so how could he sleep peacefully? Lying on the bed, he turns to sleep on his side for a while, then turns to sleep on his back for a while. Although his eyes are closed, his nerves are even more sensitive. Things he couldn't think of while awake, he now thinks of. If I marry Yang Guizhi now, then I will truly have a home. I won't have to have my father, accompanied by a servant, living in a deep courtyard, sewing and mending, cooking and doing everything himself, as if he were a wandering monk. Once a daughter-in-law enters the home, these problems will naturally be easily solved. In another two years, my father will definitely be able to hold a grandson. At that time, even if I am serving in the military away from home, someone will comfort my father. I won't have to feel like I'm constantly letting my father down, like I do now. The more he thought, the more excited he became, and the more excited he became, the more he wanted to think. He also realized a bit that if he kept thinking like this, when would it end? It wouldn't stop until dawn! If he really thought until dawn, then of course he wouldn't have any energy when he woke up tomorrow. A soldier's top priority is to be energetic. If tomorrow is inspection day, and I'm not energetic, then how can I cope with this difficult situation? I should quickly rest and conserve my energy. After I have restored my energy and overcome this difficulty, then I can proceed with the marriage in peace, that won't be too late. Tonight, the first task is still sleep, I can't think about anything else. So, he suppressed the surging thoughts in his mind and resolved to sleep. (138) The Slanting Bridge on a Summer Night Tiger Head

Shanghai was originally a paradise. Probably those who have never been to Shanghai, or those who long to come to Shanghai, have this idea. Looking at the Bund, gold and paper intoxicate the senses, it is naturally a paradise on earth, making people imagine "This place is so enjoyable, I don't want to go back to Shu." Especially at night, in the tall Western-style buildings, the electric lights are bright, and the music is enchanting. Pairs of men and women embrace each other, how pleasant, almost forgetting the hot summer. If you take a patrol to the Nanshi Slanting Bridge when you have nothing to do at night, you might suspect you have entered the gates of hell, completely contrary to the ideal paradise. Because the residents here are mostly middle-class or lower, a one- or two-story house has to accommodate six or seven families. It goes without saying that the front and back buildings and the attic are full of people... Even the kitchen lean-to and the back of the living room are full. Therefore, a house always has to let out twenty or so people. Imagine... A cage-like house, accommodating so many people, how can they sleep when it's too hot to bear? Therefore, the clever men and women have to spread broken mats on the cement to make temporary open-air beds. This open-air bed is neither as hot as a steamer nor do bedbugs and mosquitoes disturb one's dreams, making one happy and content. Then, when one person starts the trend, everyone follows. Every evening, the cement floor is already crowded with people. Although it's not yet time to sleep, they come early to reserve a spot, afraid of being beaten to the punch! Sometimes, there is a lot of bickering because of arriving late to reserve a spot. This is completely the world of coolies. They seek coolness in the summer, but when they settle the accounts in the autumn, it's mostly the coolies who suffer. A certain doctor said... "Our business is only best in the autumn." "Shanghai was originally a paradise," this statement, seen from here, becomes somewhat inaccurate... But there are still many people who desperately want to come to Shanghai. After a Hot Summer Afternoon Hu Xiaomi

The weather is extraordinarily hot, baring one's torso and vigorously waving a palm-leaf fan, beads of sweat like yellow beans still keep popping out.

In the afternoon, everything is quiet, and the stuffy weather makes people doze off.

The sky is as green and oily as the sea, far and high, as if it's boundless. There is not a hint of wind, and the tree branches stand straight and still. The sun scorches like fierce fire. Even at a distance of twenty or thirty feet, you can feel the heat radiating out.

The paulownia trees in the front yard grow tall and dense, blocking the sunlight, making the scene even more secluded and lovely. An old yellow dog lies in the shade of the tree, stretching out its tongue and panting heavily with its mouth wide open.

Outside the shade of the tree, on the scattered pieces of watermelon rind in the sunlight, many flies gather, buzzing and flying up for a while, then buzzing and settling down again, seemingly loving something delicious, wanting to give it up but unwilling to part with it.

From outside the wall comes the sound of "Sour plum soup" being hawked, with the long, drawn-out sound interspersed with the small gongs of candy sellers.

Other than that, everything is silent. Small Recipe Corn Yiqiu

"Corn," commonly known as "pearl rice" in Shanghai, "imperial rice" in the Suzhou-Yu area, and "corn" or "baogu" in the north, is an annual plant that blooms in late spring and bears fruit in summer. The fruit comes in yellow, white, red, and other colors, with both glutinous and non-glutinous varieties. It tastes sweet and fragrant, with those produced in my native Suzhou being the best. Recently, it has been appearing on the market, but most people see it as just a snack. As far as I know, it can be made into dishes and snacks, each with its own unique flavor. As "corn" comes into season, I am writing down the methods of preparation as follows to inform those who do not know.

Making Dishes

I have tried two ways of making dishes with corn... (1) Take a certain amount of fresh corn (preferably the non-glutinous type), shave off the kernels, and stir-fry them with "Beijing Dongcai" (available in southern goods stores). The taste is especially delicious. The stir-frying method is extremely simple: first, pour the shaved kernels into a pot of boiling oil, stir-fry for about half a minute, add a little soy sauce, salt, and sugar, then add the Beijing Dongcai, and add a small cup of water. The total time in the pot should be three minutes. However, there are two points to note: first, you must use high heat for stir-frying; second, the corn you use must be tender and fresh. (2) Take a whole chicken, remove the internal organs, choose half a pound of glutinous and fresh corn kernels, slowly fill the chicken's cavity, add one mace of salt, gently mix, use kelp (sold in southern goods stores) to tightly bind the chicken's body, place it in a pot of boiling water, add a spoonful of Shaoxing wine, and cook over high heat for about an hour. Then add a little salt to the soup, tightly seal the pot with wet paper, switch to charcoal embers, and simmer over low heat for about three or four hours, then it's done. The chicken meat, soup, and corn all have unique flavors. This method is available in restaurants around Tianjin and Beijing, called "Corn Chicken."

Making Snacks

The "Wo Wo Tou" that northerners love to eat is made from corn; however, southerners generally don't like the taste because of the poor preparation method. My mother grew up in Beijing and is skilled in the art of eating. After moving to Suzhou, she often made "Wo Wo Tou" as gifts for Suzhou relatives and friends, and they were greatly praised. The method has been reformed and is quite suitable for the taste of southerners. The method is as follows: Prepare the materials in advance... Sun-dried corn kernels (available at grain stores; buy them back and grind them into a fine powder), brown sugar, pine nuts, raw lard (cut into dice-sized pieces), and cold boiled water. For example, if you use three liters of corn flour, add one liter of cold boiled water and half a catty of brown sugar, stir well, and knead frequently by hand (the consistency should be the same as fresh wonton skin). Add the diced lard and pine nuts, each one or two hundred grains (the amount is not fixed), mix well, knead into the shape of a Shandong steamed bun, and dig a concave hole underneath, shaped like a stone mortar. Place it in a steamer and steam for about an hour, and it's done. The taste is very delicious, especially for those who like sweet food. Sour Plum Soup Especially

In the flourishing summer cities, fresh orange juice, ice cream, and soda water have become essential fine products, or rather, tonics. Among them, sour plum soup is the most common. Perhaps to compete (or to show authenticity), all vendors of sour plum soup must add the words "Beijing," as if without it, they would not be popular. Thus, big names like Zheng Fuzhai, and smaller ones like XX Ji or XX Zhai, are scattered throughout the cities to comfort those who are running around, thirsty and hot. Mentioning sour plum soup brings to mind something from childhood: I really enjoyed listening to others tell stories, especially those about battles in ancient times. Thus, on one occasion, I heard a story about Cao Cao's military campaign in the Three Kingdoms period, and I was naturally fascinated. He (the storyteller) said that once, Cao Cao sent troops to fight Liu Bei. On the way, there was no water to drink, and the soldiers were very thirsty, causing a great uproar. The generals also felt the same pain and found it difficult to cope, so they reported the situation to Cao Cao. Cao Cao then rode his horse forward and shouted loudly, "Are you all thirsty? Then hurry onward! There are many plum orchards ahead, enough to quench your thirst!" The soldiers heard this, their mouths watering, and they no longer felt thirsty. Although this is just a short story, we can imagine the status of "plums" at the time, and the ingenuity of improvising in ancient warfare. Now, "Beijing Sour Plum Soup" has been fully launched on the market, and drinkers are drinking it like cattle. Fortunately, the "Beijing" that is used as a slogan is still safely preserved. Now that the ceasefire has been realized, I wonder if the Northeast can still enjoy sipping as before, and whether the aftertaste of drinking is sweet or sour?

High School Examination Pass Certificates Issued to Students Who Passed All Subjects

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education announced yesterday that, after reviewing the high school graduation examination for this year, there are some students who have passed eight or six subjects and have one or three subjects that have not been examined. According to the Ministry of Education's Order No. 6559, the method for taking makeup exams and continuing education is to first apply to public and private universities, colleges, or specialized schools in this city with a certificate issued by this bureau. However, after being admitted, they must still request a makeup exam from this bureau. Only those who pass the makeup exam will be allowed to attend classes. Those who fail will have their admission qualifications revoked. Furthermore, according to the Ministry of Education's Order No. 6558, "Those who wish to apply to public and private specialized schools above the specialized school level outside of Shanghai should clearly fill in their applications when receiving the certificate and submit them to the bureau for review and notification." This bureau has decided to issue the aforementioned certificates from today until January 10th. The students may have their school, parents, or themselves fill in the admission ticket number, the school they are applying to, and submit a 2.5-inch photo to the bureau to apply for the certificate in order to apply for specialized schools and above in advance. After the bureau decides on the date of the makeup exam, they will follow the instructions and take the exam. It is hereby announced for your information. The Path That Chinese Elementary School Education Should Follow in the Future

Director Pan's Speech at the Summer School Memorial Week

Yesterday, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education's Third Summer School held a Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Director Pan Gongzhan presided over the meeting. After Director Pan led the lecturers, staff, and students in paying respects, he continued to speak about the path that Chinese elementary school education should follow in the future. He stated that the purpose of Chinese education is based on the Three Principles of the People, but the methods and training paths for guiding students in primary and secondary schools and universities should each have special points of emphasis. Secondary schools and universities will not be discussed in detail. Regarding elementary schools, the acquisition of knowledge by children should value personal activities and experiences. Neglecting the dynamic knowledge of society and life and blindly regarding textbooks as the main base of learning materials is a major shortcoming of Chinese education in the past. Those engaged in elementary school education in the future should understand that children's innate organs, such as ears, eyes, mouth, nose, etc., are all tools for children to seek knowledge. Instead of emphasizing the instillation of dead knowledge, it is better to sharpen children's various knowledge-seeking tools so that they can benefit endlessly. Finally, he said that the training path for elementary school children should focus on memory, music, and drawing. Children have a better attitude towards learning than adults, so they can easily memorize the content of learning materials. Teachers can make full use of the characteristics of children's memory to guide them to memorize the minimum amount of knowledge, while using music to harmonize their temperament and promote their national spirit, and using drawing to cultivate their ability to appreciate and observe real objects. Drawing and music are favored by children, and we should inspire children's psychological preferences and pay attention to guidance, while memorizing relevant materials, in order to cultivate the foundation of the Three Principles of the People's education. During Director Pan's speech, all the students listened attentively and quietly, and the order was orderly, which is enough to know the spirit of the bureau's summer school. The Former Middle School Joint Association Ends

The Shanghai Middle School Students' Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association had already resolved to end, and the details of its end have been reported in various newspapers, and the accounts have also been audited and published. However, the documents and equipment taken away by the Public Security Bureau have not been recovered, which has affected the inability to end some accounts. It is now learned that the person in charge of the end of the association feels that this protracted delay is not a good plan. In order to expedite the clearing of the procedures, it has been decided to entrust the Middle School Students' United Association to handle the unfinished matters. The remaining funds of the association, excluding expenses such as printing the Middle School Joint Association's special issue and advertising expenses, which are still undetermined at 60 yuan, have been transferred from the association's deposit account at the Shanghai Municipal Bank. The remaining 4,240 yuan and 5 jiao in the Shanghai Municipal Bank's deposit account have been fully transferred to the Middle School Students' United Association by Xiao Sizhi, the person in charge of the end of the association. At this point, the association has completely ended. The association is afraid that the representatives of the various schools have unclear matters that need to be inquired, and has specially stipulated that before 10:00 am on the 27th of this month, they can go to Yi Chenjun at the Far East News Agency on Luban Road to transfer to Xiao Sizhi. Overdue, they will not be responsible in order to clear the procedures. The University Teachers' Association Convened an Extraordinary Executive Committee Meeting Yesterday

Discussing the Ministry of Education's Suspension of Enrollment in Schools of Law and Political Science

The Shanghai University Faculty and Staff Union, which had previously resolved to adjourn for two months during the summer vacation, convened an extraordinary executive committee meeting yesterday morning at the union's headquarters to discuss how to deal with the recent Ministry of Education's order to suspend enrollment in law schools and political science colleges in this city. Zhang Shouyong, Kang Xuan Yi, Lin Congke, Zhang Jixin, Jiang Zhen San, Qiu Hanping, and Li Shengwu attended, and Chen Jilie and others were present. Zhang Jixin chaired the meeting, and Kang Xuanyi served as the recorder. A. Reporting Matters, (1) Committee Member Jiang Zhen San reported the reason for convening the extraordinary executive committee meeting, (2) Committee Member Chen Jilie reported the details of the Ministry of Education's suspension of enrollment in law schools and political science colleges. B. Discussion Matters, (1) How should we respond to the Ministry of Education's explicit order to suspend enrollment in law schools and political science colleges? It was resolved that the union should submit a written request to the Ministry of Education outlining the difficulties and requesting that the order be withdrawn. The Municipal Zoo is Scheduled to Open on August 1st

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education will convert the old site of Qinpu Road in Wenmiao into the Municipal Zoo, which is scheduled to officially open on August 1st. Unless there are other reasons, the date will not be changed. A reasonable fee will be charged for visitors. The annual pass is one yuan per ticket. For those who enter at any time, the fee is six copper coins, and half the fee will be charged for children. Recent News on Enrollment at National Jinan University

Today's Registration Time is Extended to 4:00 PM

National Jinan University began accepting new students for this year yesterday. In the past two days, the number of applicants to the school has been extremely enthusiastic, especially those who wish to enter the Colleges of Science and Business. The change in the aspirations of young people, focusing on science and construction, is a good phenomenon. After the merger of the Colleges of Law and Education, the school has exerted its full strength to expand the Colleges of Liberal Arts, Science, and Business. The College of Science has added more than 40,000 yuan of new instruments and specimens after the war. The equipment is quite new and complete. From the next semester, the curriculum will be revised, and experimentation and lectures will be equally emphasized. The College of Business has been established for the longest time, with more than ten years of history. Recently, the College of Business has established five departments. In addition to actively innovating the curriculum to meet the needs of international affairs, it has also made arrangements with major banks, companies, and factories in Shanghai to send students from the college to the banks, companies, and factories for practical exercises on a regular basis in order to train business talents who can adapt to domestic and foreign business wars. The College of Liberal Arts is also implementing a newly revised curriculum, not only paying attention to the cultivation of intelligence and the guidance of thought, but also emphasizing basic training to cultivate the foundation for academic research. Therefore, special attention is paid to Chinese, English, Japanese, French, German, and other languages. Recently, due to the economic depression in various overseas regions, many overseas Chinese parents feel economic difficulties, which has prevented their children from returning home to study. The school has specifically formulated preferential measures for overseas Chinese students, which have been reported in previous newspapers. President Zheng has telegraphed the preferential measures to overseas consulates, requesting that they be forwarded to overseas Chinese in various regions. Recently, the school has received telegrams from overseas requesting an extension of the deadline for the overseas Chinese student entrance examination to facilitate their return to the country for the examination. It is reported that the school has agreed to extend the deadline to before August 25. In addition, the school has been receiving too many applicants recently. For the convenience of the new students who are coming to the school to register this time, today's registration time has been extended to 4:00 PM. Recent News on Enrollment at Pudong Middle School

Since the new principal, Dr. Xu Zhi, took office at Pudong Middle School, he has been working hard to organize and improve school affairs, so the work is very tense. Film Special: The German Film Industry Under Hitler's Rule (Part 2) by Huang Junru

"Germany Awakens" was also a propaganda film for the Nazi party system and premiered on April 20th, Hitler's birthday. This film also had a subtitle called "Record of German National Regeneration" and, like "Bleeding Germany," contained a large number of speeches by Nazi brownshirts.

In addition, private film companies also catered to the wishes of the Nazi Party, producing a large number of fascist films, such as "Rhine Pathos" and other new patriotic war films. The famous director Seretti and Norman jointly announced that they would produce the national essence film "Supreme Germany." This film is expected to be divided into two parts, one called "Dance of Death" and the other "Paving the Way," using historical events from 1918 to 1933, the eve of the Nazi Party's seizure of power, as dramatic material. Goebbels has already approved of this and promised to provide strong support. Also, "Under the Black Assault Flag," which was recently shown at the Kabitel Theater, depicts farmers in East Prussia. No professional actors were used during its filming, and the roles were selected only from farmers. It takes as its theme the gradual abandonment of feudal traditions since the Middle Ages by the rural villages, weakened by the capitalist invasion after the European war and nearing starvation, and their awakening to stand under the fascist banner. The ending features a speech by Nazi leader Hitler, showing that this is a completely Nazi propaganda film.

The Hitler government is very strict with film censorship. Not only are films incompatible with the Nazi Party's claims forbidden from being shown, but the business rights of Jewish film operators are also exploited, resulting in a severe blow to the American film import industry. Among the films banned from being shown, American and Russian films are generally the most numerous, followed by French and British films. Italian films are very popular, which is due to the cooperation between Germany and Italy and the fact that both countries are fascist.

The above is a general picture of the German film industry under Hitler's iron-fisted rule. But what will the future trend be? If the Hitler government does not fall, there is no doubt that the entire German film industry will become fascist. This can be seen from the following facts: The "German Film Artists Protection Association," which encompasses all German film artists, not only merged with the Nazi Party's cultural and political organs and became a shock force for the Nazi Party's cultural movement, but also was initially controlled by the "German Culture Combat League," the mastermind behind the exclusion of Jews, and later automatically dissolved its organization (May 8) and joined the "German Culture Combat League" and the "National Party Operating Cell Organization." From then on, German film artists and technicians lost their independent position and organization and became members of the Nazi Party. Therefore, the German film industry will inevitably be painted with the colors of Hitlerism, and the films produced will undoubtedly be Nazi propaganda. (The End)

Viewer Opinions: Talking about "Two Seconds" by Mihu

European and American movies generally can't escape the story of male and female entanglements, so the romance theme in this "Two Seconds" is not worth paying attention to. However, the author of "Two Seconds" seems to be standing on a position of slight revulsion towards the current "American-style" male and female entanglements, so he consecutively used things like forced marriage after drunkenness, and frivolous beatings and frivolous repentance, to show how hasty and irresponsible modern men and women are towards marriage.

Secondly, the producer is very clear about the greatness of the power of money, so he not only writes that Shirley still associates with the dance hall manager Turner even after marrying John, but he also writes that after John gets sick, John's wife borrows money from Turner, the person John hates the most. Although they were lucky enough to win the lottery and pay off their debts, Shirley was still beaten to death, and "the forensic doctor did not allow the criminal to defend himself and carried out the death penalty according to the院长's order." This passage gives no small amount of satire to the current law.

As for the technical aspect, I must first introduce the flashback method in this film. The death row inmate John repents for two seconds in the electric chair, and the entire story unfolds in John's memory. Flashbacks, or recall methods, are common in movies. However, whether it is possible to recall such detail in the short time of two seconds, no one really knows.

Editor's Note: The film "Two Seconds" was shown at the Cathay Theater more than two months ago. This is the second time it has been re-screened at the Carlton, so there is no need to comment on it again. However, the points raised by Mr. Mihu are insightful, so I have presented them specifically. As for recalling so many things in two seconds, I think it's impossible. I think "a sudden impulse, a moment of sadness" is the most that could happen. But I dare not be too assertive, or perhaps when sitting in the electric chair, thoughts turn faster, that is also unknown.

Not Clever: A Tit for Tat by Xifu

John Barrymore is a big star from a family of performers. Because he is a big star, he is very proud. Because he is so proud, he is inevitably a bit arrogant. Many movie fans who admire stars like to ask the stars to sign their names, just like people in our country ask for calligraphy from great men and teachers. But when they meet John Barrymore, they are rejected by him. So many people are afraid to take liberties because Barrymore is so arrogant. But not long ago, a great thinker, playwright, writer, and barbarian head came to Hollywood. He is none other than the famous George Bernard Shaw. This time, it was something! John Barrymore hosted a banquet to welcome Shaw. These two big brains in the theater and film industry, although the host and guests were friendly and harmonious, couldn't help but have a sense of testing each other in their hearts when heroes meet. John Barrymore first took a book and said to the old man Shaw, "This is my son's book, please sign it so that the child's wishes may be fulfilled." Old man Shaw smiled and patted Barrymore on the shoulder, saying, "If this book were your grandfather's, I would sign it for him." When this news spread, everyone who had always felt that John Barrymore was arrogant applauded and cheered, because old man Shaw had avenged them.

One Type of Star's Pastime by Fu

Some Can Use It, Some Can't

Gloria Swanson recently invented a pastime. When she has nothing to do, she picks up the telephone and makes calls for fun. She has no purpose in making calls. She randomly picks a number in the telephone book and dials it. Her intention is to tell the person who answers the phone that she is Gloria Swanson, and listen to the other person's surprised voice: "Oh!" Then she chats casually for a while to kill time. The people who answer the phone are also very happy, and many people hope to have this good fortune one day, to receive a call from Swanson.

Later, Little Fairbanks heard about this pastime, and he also imitated it. One day, when he had nothing to do, he picked up the phone and started making calls in his bedroom. The person who answered the phone was a little girl. Little Fairbanks thought, great, it's also good to talk to a child. So he told her that he was Little Fairbanks. He waited for a while, but there was no reply on the other end. He said again, "I am Little Fairbanks, did you hear me?" From then on, Little Fairbanks never dared to make phone calls for fun again.

Many Stars Go to Europe by Fu

Babe Daniels has already gone to Europe. She wants to make a film in London, England. Sally Eilers also went with her. She didn't have any purpose in going, but was just accompanying Babe Daniels for fun. Later, after they arrived in England, the British Gaumont Company also hired Sally Eilers, so now Sally is also making films in England. Pascal recently took a ship to Europe. He will also be making films in England soon, and his wife will also be going to England soon. Now Hollywood is also rumored that Maurice Chevalier will be going to Europe soon. He wants to return to France by ship after his contract with Paramount expires. He wants to shoot a musical film himself in France.

Garbo's Old Temper Hasn't Changed by Fu

People say that Greta Garbo's temper has changed since she returned to Hollywood from Europe, and she is not as eccentric as before. But that's wrong, her temper hasn't changed at all. On her first day in America, she would talk and laugh, and she would stand and let reporters take pictures. She also said a few words to greet the reporters gathered at the dock. But since she got in the car and returned to Hollywood, she has returned to her old temper. She now, except for work, does not meet with reporters, does not allow people to take pictures, and is as eccentric as before. She is now asking the company to call Ronald Colman back to be her supporting actor, but Colman is now in Europe and probably won't be able to return for a while.

The Dark World of Hollywood by Bing

A type of bathroom is now popular in Hollywood, and many stars are imitating it in their homes. The interior of this type of bathroom is completely black. The walls are made of black mica stone, the bathtub is made of black porcelain, the chairs are also black, the floor is also black, the washbasin is even more black, even the soap is black, and the towels are also black. Even the bathrobe must be black. In short, everything is black. Many stars have specially hired black people dressed in black clothes, black shoes, and black socks to manage this black bathroom.

When Greta Garbo was in Europe, she heard that Hollywood had discovered the dark world and found it very interesting. She said to her friends, "Everything is black in the bathroom, but it would be best if the water was also black, then after bathing in the dark bathroom with black water, everyone could become black people."

A Recent Photo of Mae West, Whose Plump Figure is Temporarily Fashionable

London Silver Screen Stars by Luo Fen

Following the Thousand-Faced Man Lon Chaney, Boris Karloff, who sacrificed himself for art, has risen to fame since playing in "Frankenstein." Recently, after Boris played in "The Mummy," he was deeply praised by the British film industry, and Gaumont Company hired him.

Charles Laughton left for Europe immediately after playing in Paramount's "The Private Life of Henry VIII" because he had no contractual constraints. He is now in London, dressed in the clothes of King Henry VIII in the 1570s. He goes to Hampton Court Palace to play every day. He is a descendant of the British royal family, so he can enter and exit the palace. He is now in London, and may join the Gaumont Company. Gaumont Company has sent people to contact him.

Samuel Goldwyn and his wife, the bosses of MGM, have now arrived in London. Samuel Goldwyn is now the world's leading film magnate. The British film industry also admires Goldwyn's methods of reforming the film industry. This time, Samuel Goldwyn and his wife arrived in London. The London film industry held a grand welcome party for them, and many Londoners participated in the welcome, which was quite grand for a while.

Tour of European and American Film Studios (6) by Yun Yan

The Universal City employs a total of 1,000 people. There is a zoo inside with lions, elephants, tigers, leopards, and everything else. There is also a chicken farm with about thousands of chickens. There are stables inside with many horses. When Western films (i.e., martial arts films) were popular, many cowboys also lived in the studio. There is also an entertainment hall for employees with very good facilities. There is a large restaurant where people from outside can also eat.

Before 1915, Universal Pictures was filming in a very small studio. This studio was in the middle of Gower and Baily Wood, and it has long been burned down. At that time, Carl Laemmle, seeing that the film business would definitely develop in the future, began to build today's large studio. After it was completed, more than 45,000 people sat on special buses to see this strange place. Even Edison and Henry Ford drove their cars there to visit.

Universal Studio, in the era of silent films, was of course very powerful. A group of the earliest big stars, such as May Murray and Lon Chaney, were famous in Universal. Since the popularity of sound films, it has also grown rapidly and entered a new front.

All the equipment and machinery in the studio have been replaced with the latest models.

(British) Beaconsfield Film Studio

The British Lion Film Corporation Studio in Buckinghamshire, England

Beaconsfield is located in Buckinghamshire. It is a completely British town. The town has a wide crossroads. The houses at the head of the street are still lifeless at noon, as if they are sleeping there. Only after the British Lion Film Corporation was established did the town gradually become lively. Now, the mothers of Beaconsfield will also bring their babies to the studio to act as extras. The children of Beaconsfield will also go to see how those movie stars work.

This studio is hidden under a very high roof. Its bottom layer has a large area. On the side of this large building, there is a row of bungalows that are the workshops for plasterers and carpenters. On the other side, there is a film projection room, office, and a row of places to store films. The entire studio is located on a large lawn, surrounded by very high walls. (To be continued)

Shen Bao Third Sheet 164

Assassination of Prime Minister Inukai

Military Court Opens Trial 165

Hualian News Agency, 24th, Tokyo Telegraph - The Japanese Navy opened a military court at the Yokosuka Naval Base at 9:00 AM this morning to try the ten assassins, including Lieutenant Commander Koga, in the assassination of Prime Minister Inukai. The court will convene every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday, with thirty sessions scheduled to complete the trial. The number of spectators is limited to thirty. After the court opens, a ban on public attendance will be announced. The army assassins are scheduled to be tried in a military court in Tokyo tomorrow, with the trial expected to conclude in twelve days.

Hualian News Agency, 24th, Tokyo Telegraph - The naval assassins in the May 15th assassination of Prime Minister Inukai case in Japan were tried in a military court this morning. The details are as follows:

Heavy Guard Along the Way - The eleven naval assassins awaiting trial departed from the Otsu Prison at 8:00 AM this morning, traveling in three cars to the Kusunoura Military Court. A truck carrying ten armed police officers led the way in front of the three cars. Behind them, two more trucks, each carrying twelve police officers, followed. Police Inspector Nagareishi and Police Inspector Koiso led fifty-three police officers to guard both sides of the road. Military Police Sergeant Major Tazuke led seven military police officers, and Warden Murakami led six wardens, accompanying the assassins. They arrived at the court at 8:15 AM. Lieutenant Commander Tsukano sat on the right, and the others were seated according to their military rank, awaiting the start of the trial. All the assassins wore white naval service uniforms.

Defendants Tried Separately - The May 15th case involved assassins from the army, navy, and civilian sectors. The trials are being conducted separately. The navy defendants, considered the masterminds, are being tried first. The testimonies of the assassins are drawing significant attention from all sides. The judges for the naval military court are: Presiding Judge, Navy Captain Takasu Shiro; Judges, Navy Lieutenant Commander Owada Noboru, Lieutenant Kihara Yoshitane, and Lieutenant Fujio Katsuo. The legal officers for this case are Takarai Osamu (legal counsel) and Shiosui Shigetoshi (prosecutor). This is the complete list of those conducting the trial. There are eleven assassins in total, charged with three different types of crimes. Those charged with the crime of rebellion are Navy Lieutenant Commander Koga Kiyoshi, Nakamura Yoshio, Mikami Taku, Yamagishi Hiroshi, Navy Reserve Ensign Kuroiwa Isamu, and Ensign Murakami Kakunosuke. Those charged with the crime of preparing for rebellion are Navy Lieutenant Commander Tsukano Michio,

Lieutenant Hayashi Masayoshi, Ensign Ito Kameki, and Oba Haruo, a total of eleven people. The five lawyers are Kiyose Ichiro, Doctor of Laws and Secretary-General of the National Alliance, Fukuda Kurabunji, Hayashi Itsuro, Navy Lieutenant Asada, and Navy Lieutenant Shimizu.

Reading of the Charges Against the Accused - Before the assassins entered the courtroom, the spectator seats were already full. News reporters and families of the assassins were present. In the special spectator seats, Commander Nomura, Chief of Staff Hamada, Director of the Eda Naval Air Arsenal, Director of the Military Affairs Bureau of the Navy Ministry Terashima, Director of the Education Bureau Goto, Director of the Legal Affairs Bureau Yamada, and Director of the Murata Naval Arsenal, totaling about twenty people, sat behind the judges. The lawyers sat on both sides of the assassins. At 9:25 AM, Presiding Judge Takasu announced the opening of the court. The prosecutor read the charges against each defendant as follows: "The defendants were influenced and guided by the late Navy Lieutenant Commander Fujii Hitoshi. Lieutenant Commander Fujii, while at the Naval Academy, advocated Pan-Asianism, seeking to unite the Asian nations with Japan as their leader, in order to punish the violence of the white races and spread morality to the world. Defendants Koga Kiyoshi and Murayama Kakunosuke, under his leadership, worked to gather comrades, instigating defendants Ito Kameki and Hayashi Masayoshi to convene a meeting of a dozen people, including Murayama, Ito, and Oba, in the Dansui Pavilion in Tsuchiura Town in July of Showa 5 (1930) to discuss organizing a direct action group. In February of the same year, they gathered more than a dozen people, including Mikami, Koga, and Murayama, at the Kashi Hot Springs in Fukuoka Prefecture to hold a meeting to discuss organizing a group to reform national politics through direct action. After Lieutenant Commander Fujii died in battle in Shanghai, the defendants did not change their original intentions. Koga Kiyoshi and Nakamura Yoshio, as leaders, continued his goals, disturbing the peace of the imperial capital through collective direct action, intending to create a state of martial law, and under martial law, to seek the reform of the nation. Therefore, the public prosecution is brought against each defendant on the aforementioned charges."

Lieutenant Commander Koga's Testimony 166

Hualian News Agency, 24th

Tokyo Telegraph - In the military court today, Lieutenant Commander Koga replied to Presiding Judge Takasu, stating, "My motivation for participating in the May 15th Incident was that while studying at the Naval Academy, I was moved by Lieutenant Commander Fujii's Pan-Asianism. Later, I became acquainted with Inoue Nissho. In Taisho 14, I was introduced by Fujii, and Dr. Okawa became our teacher and comrade. Inoue Nissho is the central figure in this case. Both the army and navy were guided by him. As for Gondo Seikyo, he was not our comrade, but he showed great sympathy for our movement. The assassination of Lieutenant Commander Nishida was due to suspicion that he had betrayed us. I was greatly guided in my thinking by Fujii, but during my time at the Naval Academy, I was also greatly inspired by Toyama Mitsuru's instructions from Saigo Takamori, which stated, 'Only those who do not fear death or fame can accomplish great things.' The 'Chankanjo' (petition for justice) regarding the assassination of Asahi of the Yasuda Zaibatsu also greatly stimulated my thinking. Regarding the London Naval Treaty, Japanese representative Zaibu was the son-in-law of Yamamoto, the Satsuma clique admiral, and colluded with the zaibatsu, forgetting the navy's position and blindly following Wakatsuki Reijiro. Although he was a naval officer, he had very little support within the navy. The purpose of the meetings in May of Showa 5 and spring of Showa 6 was to plan the reformation of national politics. The matters discussed at that time were telegraphed to Lieutenant Commander Fujii, who expressed opposition. The method agreed upon at the time was to adopt the principle of 'kill one to save one' and a plan to attack the Shinbunsha (newspaper company). The process was the same as described in the investigation. I wish to state the truth of the ○○ incident to clarify this case." Presiding Judge Takasu stated that this case would disrupt peace and order and therefore prohibited spectators. At 2:00 PM, the secret trial resumed. Lieutenant Commander Koga detailed the truth. The so-called ○○ incident is rumored to be the Nishiki-e Revolution Incident of mid-October of Showa 6. This case will continue tomorrow."

The Lion of Flanders 167

Dies in Berlin

Built Extraordinary Achievements During the European War

Kokumin, 23rd, Berlin Telegraph - German Navy Admiral Schroeder, famous as "The Lion of Flanders," died in Berlin today at the age of seventy-nine. During the European War, Schroeder commanded the naval base in northern Belgium and guarded the German army's right flank, which controlled the English Channel. Schroeder planned to attack the British coast with submarines and bomb London from the sky.

Large Conspiracy of the Japan Production Party Uncovered (Japan News) 168

丨The Great Assassination Plan of the Divine Soldiers Was Not Implemented丨

On the surface, domestic Japan, since the incident on May 15th last year when active-duty officers of the army and navy brazenly shot and killed Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi in broad daylight, and after the military and government cooperated to appease the situation, the unrest has not continued to escalate. The actions of the left wing are naturally subject to severe suppression by the law and the police under the guidance of the law. There is only underground activity, and daily struggles are only slightly expressed in the economic and cultural aspects. However, the various right-wing groups are very different. They have considerable middle-class capitalists as financial backers and the army and navy as political supporters. Therefore, even if the government intends to limit their activities, its power cannot reach the military. Therefore, the activities of right-wing groups are still very vigorous and powerful. Although, strictly speaking, their actions are illegal, their movement has the tacit consent of the military and receives direct assistance from veterans' associations. Even many active-duty officers join, turning around and providing them with weapons. Therefore, the right-wing movement displayed a very strange power last year. The head of the financial cliques, Tadanuma Takuma, the key figure of the political parties, Inoue Junnosuke, and the current Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi were all assassinated one after another. This shows that the rise of the right-wing movement is not necessarily for the benefit of the Japanese rulers.

Moreover, although most of Japan's right-wing groups call themselves "Japanese Spirit," their starting point is always dissatisfaction with the current situation in Japan. They express extreme anger at the general situation in Japan, both politically and economically. In particular, after Japan invaded Manchuria, the general suffering of the Japanese people, the suffering of life, the suffering of unemployment, and the stagnation of the rural economy have not improved compared with before the September 18th Incident. The quasi-wartime military expenses are added to the general public in the name of public bonds. As a result, the people's resentment is deepening, and the lurking crisis is growing. The movement of right-wing groups is trending towards radicalism, using the guise of legality to implement terrorist policies against political authorities, supporters of parliamentary politics, and financial cliques.

Therefore, an extremely uneasy sense of terror has arisen in major cities such as Tokyo and Osaka. In particular, those responsible officials (except for military officers), financial cliques, and political party leaders are all on high alert, fearing that disaster will strike.

The Great Japan Production Party is a group of extreme elements in the right-wing groups. Their actions are extremely激越. They take direct action against the current government. In order to maintain secrecy, they do not hold cadre meetings in advance, nor do they adopt a collegiate system. They only gather a small number of cadres to plan their work. They maintain absolute secrecy about all future plans, and they do not easily let outsiders know even about the work they have implemented. Unexpectedly, their plans were uncovered by the police authorities.

Under the command of the Production Party, there is an organization called the Divine Soldiers. This Divine Soldier is the vanguard of the extreme elements. Their only method is "one person assassinating one person." This time, Suzuki Zen'ichi, the Minister of the Youth Party of the Production Party, suddenly issued an emergency call and gathered at the "Jingu Kōkaikan" of the "Meiji Jingu" at 12:00 PM on the 10th of this month to secretly plot an uprising. When the police saw this group of people, they immediately reported it to the Superintendent General of Police. Then the "Harajuku Police Station" ordered the police to be mobilized and arrested all the participants, totaling

eleven people. Only then did they learn about their plan, which was to first attack a certain gunpowder shop in Tokyo at 11:00 AM on July 11th to obtain pistols, bombs, and other weapons, and then divide into three teams. The first team leader was Maeda Miyao, and the chief of staff was Suzuki Zen'ichi. The goal was to attack the Prime Minister's residence, assassinate Prime Minister Saito Makoto, and then assassinate the ministers of the various departments. The second team was led by Uchimura Oka Kiyozō, and the goal was to surround the police and various police stations to incapacitate the police, so that Tokyo would immediately fall into a state of anarchy. The third team, led by Kageyama Seiji, first destroyed the Seiyukai, Minseito, and Kokumin Domei clubs, and then assassinated Count Makino Nobuaki, Suzuki Kisaburo, President of the Seiyukai, Wakatsuki Reijiro, President of the Minseito, and other financial cliques. They were all preparing to eliminate them all at once, but they did not know that the plan was not confidential and was recognized eleven hours before. It was defeated nine hours

before, otherwise Tokyo would have suffered a very big mess again.

Currently, the case is still under investigation. However, those in charge of the army and navy have officially stated that the military has nothing to do with this and called on everyone to rest assured. The unprecedented big case has finally been temporarily resolved. (July 19th, Tokyo)

Communist Bandits Invade the Border of Jiangxi 169

Fierce Fighting Near Xunwu

The Bandits Were Overwhelmed and Retreated in Two Directions

Guangzhou Correspondence - The Southern Route Suppression Army has been in contact with the communist bandits for several days. Government troops are using aircraft to bomb the bandit fortifications. According to reports, the pseudo-135th Army Corps in the bandit area is divided into central and northeastern Jiangxi. The pseudo-1st Army Corps is gathered south of Xingan, and the pseudo-35th Army Corps is concentrated in Yihuang. The number is said to be about 100,000 people, but in reality, each regiment has only eight or nine hundred people. Firearms account for about 60%, and the rest hold knives and spears to help and shout. The main force of the communist bandits closest to the defense zone of the Southern Route Army is the defense zone of the 1st Division of the 1st Army. The Lee Division is stationed between Ganzhou and Wan'an, close to Yongfeng and Xingan. The front line has been ordered to strictly defend against it. Therefore, the situation in the central part of the Southern Route Army has become tight recently. As for the right-wing line, the communist bandits are encroaching southward. Recently, a large number of bandit soldiers have been transferred from the pseudo-35th and 2 Army Corps to suddenly attack the vicinity of Xunwu and Anyuan. On the Xunwu side, the Ouyang Xin Department of the 22nd Regiment of the Southern Route Army was the first to make contact, and fierce battles occurred near Xunwu. Places have been lost and regained several times. The Zhang Meixin Division of the First Column and the Gui Army Wang Zanbin Department blocked the rear of the communist bandits from the vicinity of Anyuan. A part of the Independent First Division was transferred to block and suppress them. However, the climate in the Xunwu area has been hot recently, and many soldiers in the Southern Route Army are sick. The 7th Division in the area is currently setting up a temporary hospital in Dazhexu, and the 8th Division is also setting up a hospital in Sanbiaoxu to accommodate them. In the Sannan area, the Division and the Gui Army have recently been searching for communist bandits. After the great battle near Xunwu, traces of bandits were also found in places such as Chongshengxu. According to a telegram from the front line on the 15th, the red bandit pseudo-special agent company opened from Shashe on the 13th and haunted Shanglian, more than 20 miles east of Anyuan City, forcing the villagers to cut rice. The Wang Zanbin Division in the area immediately sent the Liu Battalion of the Zhou Hunyuan Regiment to search and suppress them on the morning of the 14th. At about 5:00 AM on the 15th, they came into contact with seventy or eighty communist bandits near Sunwu and fought fiercely for a while. The bandits began to flee to Sun Gao, Hou Gao Mountain. There are no traces of bandits in Shanglian, and the battalion has led the team back to defense. Also, a remnant of bandits near Xunwu was intercepted by the Zhang Meixin Division and retreated in two directions through the area of Banjianshan Chongshi: one retreated from Longbu, and the other entered Huichang from Gaopai. The 5th Air Squadron of the Southern Route Army in the East River has made contact with the aircraft squadron of the 19th Route Army of Fujian, and they are scheduled to bomb the bandit nests separately to assist the army's progress. (July 20th)

Hail Disaster in Shaanxi Province 170

＝Summer Grain Harvest Is Very Poor, and Autumn Crops Are Already Hopeless＝

Xi'an Correspondence - The disaster situation in Shaanxi Province has become more serious recently. The summer harvest is extremely poor, and the autumn harvest is still far away. Unexpectedly, recently, various counties have been hit by repeated wind, frost, and hail, and the autumn crops have been almost completely destroyed, making the scene even more tragic and forming a disaster again. The disaster situation in various counties is recorded together below.

Jingbian 171

Jingbian has received two inches of rain since March 15th and has been dry for more than two months. The people are worried about drought again. Fortunately, it rained on June 1st and 2nd. The people replanted the seedlings that had been frosted and rolled by the wind. Unexpectedly, just as the seedlings were about to emerge from the soil, there were thunderstorms again on the 16th, 17th, 18th, and 19th of this month, causing flooding on the ground. The water depth on the flat ground was one foot, so the crops on the mountainside, beams, and other places were all flooded. There is still water that has not dried and soaked the soil. Even if the water recedes in a day or two, it will still not be possible to plant. Even if it can be planted, it will only be buckwheat.

Yichuan 172

In Yichuan, there was thunder and heavy rain on the afternoon of the 10th of this month, lasting for about a quarter of an hour.

It stopped suddenly. The next day, villagers reported that there had been a severe hail disaster in the northeast of the first district. On the afternoon of the 11th, hail and rain fell intermittently for about a quarter of an hour. The large ones were the size of peaches, the small ones were the size of apricots, and some were as small as soybeans. The accumulation on the ground was an inch thick. The leaves of the trees were all fallen, and the damage to the crops can be imagined. According to statistics, there are more than 20 villages where the disaster was too severe. We have received letters from various districts reporting that there is a risk of hail, with the first district being the worst. In addition, the hail disaster in the third district is also very serious.

Xizhen 173

Heavy rains have been falling frequently here recently. At dawn on the 12th of this month, the rain continued to fall, and it only cleared at about 7:00 AM on the 13th. Around 12:00 PM, dark clouds gathered, thunder rumbled, lightning flashed, and heavy rain poured down. Low-lying areas suddenly became marshes. It only stopped slightly at about 1:00 PM in the afternoon. Also, in the vicinity of this town, there have been continuous torrential rains for days, mountain floods have erupted, and floods have mixed with the ditches, with water heads of more than 30 feet already. The crops in the ditches and the Water God Temple were all submerged. Farmers cried bitterly and complained incessantly, making people who saw them unable to hold back their tears.

Fugou 174

Since the hail fell in this county a few days ago, the climate has been unsettled, with strong winds blowing, flying dust and flying dust, making it difficult for pedestrians to find their way, and even uprooting trees. The crops in the fields were almost completely destroyed. After the gale, heavy rain poured down, lightning flashed, and thunder rumbled incessantly, falling harder and harder, like a downpour. By the 12th, the accumulated water was several feet deep. The general public was pessimistic about this gale and rain.

Jia County 175

In more than ten villages, including Guanjia Guangou and Sunjia Zhua in the southern district of this county, a hurricane suddenly rose in the middle of this month, covering the sky and the earth, with sand and stones flying, making it impossible to see anything within a foot. Two days later, the wind stopped, but there was heavy rain again, with hail mixed in, as large as peaches and apricots, falling to the ground with a sound. The crops in the fields were all broken: the larger ones had their leaves cut and their stems broken, and the smaller ones were buried in the mud. The autumn and summer crops were all destroyed. The farmers in these villages suffered this strange disaster of wind and frost and complained incessantly.

Yanchuan 176

Since May, there have been frequent gales and rainstorms here, and even hail mixed with snow. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 19th of this month, dark clouds covered the sky, the wind was very strong, and the thunder rumbled. In a moment, heavy rain poured down, with wind and hail mixed in, the large ones like eggs and peaches, the small ones like apricots and dates, lasting for dozens of minutes, with an accumulation of hail of an inch or so. The affected areas include more than 30 villages, including Beiyuan Village, Yuanze River, Dongjia Yuan, Yangjia, Majia River, Lijia Gegeng, Doujia River, Yangjia Gegeng, Louer River, Pangjia Yuan, Nanyuan Cunhe, Doujia Yuan, and Shihe Village, covering an area of over a hundred miles. Currently, the crops and trees in the fields have all withered, and the farmers are all desperate. The land is barren for thousands of miles, and the general farmers are all crying to the sky and grabbing the ground.
